Japanese Assassination Case Exposes Secrets of the Military

Military comrades not only plotting to assassinate political parties and zaibatsu

Even military factions within the military were planned to be purged.

Assassination Attempt on Minister of the Imperial Household Makino Fails

Den Tsushin dispatch of the 30th from Tokyo: The second public trial of the Blood Pledge Assassination Group incident opened at 9:00 AM today in the Tokyo District Court courtroom. Inoue Nissho said, "We do not aim to assassinate merely for the sake of assassination; this is only a means. My comrades tend to protect me. If it were not for this Inoue, then this incident and the May 15th incident would not have occurred." His response was different from the previous one and was quite spirited. At 10:00 AM, the interrogation of Furuichi began. After stating his relationship with Inoue and others, Furuichi replied, "On January 31, Showa 7, in an empty house near the residence of Gondo Seikyo, it was decided to assassinate twenty prominent figures in the political and financial worlds, and Inoue was requested to carry out this assassination task at Gondo's residence." At noon, there was a recess. The court reopened at 1:30 PM and questioned Shibamoto Yoshitaka. The defendant stated his resume, saying that he had transferred from the Seventh High School to the Imperial University and had known his ideology since meeting Inoue Nissho, which he deeply respected. He approved of the claim to reform the country, accepted the task of assassinating Minister of the Imperial Household Makino, and sought opportunities. The guard at Minister Makino's residence was severe, and he realized that one person was of no help. Therefore, he consulted with Inoue, and Tagura Yoshiyuki helped him. On February 10, Showa 7, he received a Browning pistol with fifty bullets from Inoue Nissho and delivered it to Tagura. He lodged at the Mita Inn near Minister Makino's residence to investigate the movements of the Minister. He also said that after Shohei assassinated former Minister Inoue Junnosuke, he ordered Tagura and Mori Kenkichi to return to Kyoto to deceive the ears of the authorities. Furthermore, he stated that the comrades in the military not only planned to purge the political parties and zaibatsu, but also the military factions with improper and unjust forces within the military, thus exposing the secrets of the military. Finally, he said, "Now I realize that others and I are really no different, and I deny all revolutions rooted in the concept of opposition. Now, I only have to complete myself and be filled with the desire to live." Unlike Inoue Nissho and Furuichi, he returned to idealism and expressed his remorse. At this point, today's public trial ended, and the court was adjourned at 4:10 PM. The next public trial is scheduled for July 3 to continue the hearing.

Japan United Press dispatch of the 30th from Tokyo: The second public trial of the Blood Pledge Assassination Group conspiracy incident opened at 9:00 AM today. The security was still tight. The judge originally planned to question the defendant Furuichi about the facts of the crime, but the defendant Inoue suddenly requested to speak, saying that the Navy victim and other comrades, because I harmed their health, wanted to reduce my responsibility. However, I believe that if there were no Inoue, the May 15th incident would not have occurred. I am not afraid of anything, and I practice the spirit of breaking down the privileged class, leading me to this day. Therefore, the responsibility for this case rests entirely on me.

Changes in Japanese Foreign Policy (Japan News)

Japan has recently experienced a huge change in its foreign policy, which is to abandon its long-time friend Britain and openly advocate friendship with its imaginary enemy, the United States. The fact that India, Australia, and other places have successively boycotted Japanese goods has already been clearly demonstrated. It is feared that in the future, all British Empire territories and autonomous territories will use higher tariffs to restrict the import of Japanese textiles and other manufactured goods. Japan then uses not buying Indian cotton and Australian wool as a boycott, but this boycott does not seem to be able to restore the goodwill of India and other autonomous territories and colonies under the leadership of the British Empire towards Japan, but instead provokes greater anger, making the Japanese foreign market feel a huge threat. If it is really implemented, then the Japanese textile industry, which is relatively excellent in the East, will suffer a great blow. Therefore, the business circles of Japan have been meeting everywhere in important cities such as Tokyo, Osaka, and Kobe to plan countermeasures, but until now, they have not found a real and effective method that can be implemented. They only use not buying Indian cotton and not buying wool as a passive resistance.

Politically, Britain and Japan have many of the same interests and places where they need to cooperate, especially in dealing with the Soviet Union and blocking its development to the east. Secondly, in their China policy, they also have the same position in suppressing China's national revolution, upward development, and acting in a united step, but recently the Soviet Union's foreign policy has shifted to peaceful conservatism, and Britain is therefore relieved that its interests in India and the Persian oil fields will not be in danger. At the same time, regarding China's market relations, Britain also clearly sees Japan's radicalism, because at first Japan only said that it was protecting the vested interests of "Manchuria" and volunteered to be the international vanguard against communism, so Britain acquiesced in its military action, but recently Japan has not only turned Manchuria into a second Korea, but also seized Jehol and probed into eastern Hebei, and wants to take control of Tianjin

Tokyo Smallpox Epidemic

(Reuters, Tokyo, 30th) Smallpox is currently spreading in Tokyo, so approximately one million people have been forced to be vaccinated in the past few days. When the disease was first discovered, it was mistakenly identified as chickenpox, leading to a rampant spread, with 56 people now infected. Two elementary schools have been closed as a preventative measure.

The Japanese are creating a second puppet regime, calling people like Li Jichun and Zhao Lei, Shi Fengming, to come forward. They will first establish empty titles such as Commander-in-Chief Headquarters and General Headquarters, while Japanese reserve officers and generals will command from behind. If successful, they will invade North China. Even if they fail, they can at least use it as a bargaining chip to reduce tariffs. Naturally, those with interests in the Kailuan coal mines and the Beining Railway will witness this situation, and British interests in North China will be shaken. Moreover, the Japanese army stationed in the three northeastern provinces and Rehe is also preparing to sweep Inner Mongolia and Chahar.

Therefore, the political relationship between Britain and Japan has shifted from alliance to separation. If Japan completely loses British assistance, and even faces tariff restrictions on Japanese goods throughout the British Empire, should that truly happen, Japan will fall from nominal isolation to substantial economic isolation. This is what Japan fears most, especially given its current dire economic situation. However, Japan cannot adopt the same means against Britain as it does against China. So, what will it do? For an immediate solution, Japan understands that the United States is busy resolving its domestic issues and is not very active in the Pacific power struggle. Furthermore, the investment and export trade to the Chinese market differ in quality and quantity. Japan mainly exports light industrial products to China, followed by marine products, while the United States mainly exports heavy industrial products. Although agricultural products have suddenly increased recently due to special circumstances, the trade relationship between the United States and China is not as sharply opposed as that between Japan and Britain. There is still some room for reconciliation between Japan and the United States. For example, Japan needs steel, coal, and oil, while the United States needs raw silk, etc. There is a possibility of achieving reconciliation in economics. Therefore, since the issue of India's increased tariffs arose, some Japanese have shifted from anti-American rhetoric to pro-American arguments. Even those who previously advocated war against the United States are now silent. The first step in this transformation is to break the current deadlock, eliminate the traces of the Republican administration's policies towards Japan, and start with diplomacy. When Matsuoka Yosuke visited the United States, he laid the groundwork and tried his best to seek understanding from the Democratic leaders towards Japan. Now they are planning to have Matsukata Kojiro or Matsuoka Yosuke replace Debuchi Katsuji as the ambassador to the United States, which will open a new chapter in Japanese-American diplomacy. However, the timeframe of this situation is very short. The interests between Japan and the United States cannot ultimately be harmonized, but it is a way to seek temporary stability at the moment. Therefore, Japan's policy towards China must also change. (June 21st)

Current Commentary

The Two North China Problems

Regarding the North China issue after the signing of the truce agreement, the most recent matters attracting public attention are: first, how to resolve the problem of the puppet troops rampaging in the demilitarized zone; and second, how to deal with the situation in Chahar after Feng Yuxiang raised the banner of resistance against Japan. The former could have been viewed as a domestic bandit suppression incident, but recently it has become necessary to discuss solutions with the military representatives who are manipulating them from behind. The latter appears to be an action of resisting the enemy and defending against aggression, but recently its focus has shifted to domestic political relations. Although the nature of the two issues is different, the authorities in Beiping, considering the complexity of the content of the issues, are trying to resolve them through peaceful means. Their efforts are also well-intentioned.

People like Li Jichun and Zhao Lei are manipulated by the Japanese to disrupt various places in eastern Hebei, and at the same time, they use the name of the anti-Japanese army to conceal their relationship with the Japanese. Even on the surface, they are neither Chinese nor Japanese, but simply bandits who have risen opportunistically. Northern commentators, based on the principles of the truce agreement, advocate clarifying the status of Li Zhao and others with the Japanese in order to resolve the issue. They believe that if the Japanese army admits that the puppet troops are part of their force that invaded the Great Wall, they should withdraw to the line of the Great Wall according to the agreement. If they consider them unrelated, they should allow the Chinese army to suppress them. Although this is merely theoretical, it is still a suggestion that could facilitate the resolution of the puppet troop problem. If, as reported by newspapers and telegrams recently, the puppet troops have achieved their goal of being incorporated and are allowed to remain in eastern Hebei, then even if the problem is resolved, the hidden dangers will remain. Such a resolution will still leave behind some problems, so the authorities' hard work in handling this matter is known to us. Making compromises to avoid the emergence of complications is also out of necessity. However, after the incorporation, the authorities should plan early on how to transform them into a security police force that is somewhat reliable and how to ensure that their continued presence in the area does not hinder the takeover of various places, in order to avoid future disputes.

When the truce negotiations were underway, Feng Yuxiang, knowing that the people's anger towards foreign aggression was increasing, declared armed protection of Chahar Province and began his extraordinary actions. Whether this kind of action is appropriate or not can be temporarily set aside. However, since May 26th, after more than a month, the people have not seen his achievements in resisting the war, and they cannot help but have doubts about his so-called "only helping to lead his troops to fight against foreign aggression and never seek to establish a separatist regime." If we compare the excitement of the people towards Ma Zhanshan's resistance against Japan in Heilongjiang Province and the enthusiastic assistance to the 19th Route Army's defense against the enemy in Shanghai with today's attitude towards the Chahar incident, we cannot simply feel emotional about Feng's situation. The recent impasse in Chahar lies in Feng's unwillingness to leave Zhangjiakou, causing Song Zheyuan to be unable to return to Chahar. We believe that the personal matter of Feng's stay or departure is small. If the various armies can, as stated in his telegraphs, sincerely work to recover the lost territory before launching an attack, then it seems that there would be no difficult problems for Song Zheyuan to lead his troops back to the town. The resolution of the Chahar situation also seems difficult but is actually easy. What we cannot help but feel emotional about is that the saying that the national crisis is profound is on everyone's lips, but today's North China is preoccupied with these kinds of problems, attracting the attention of the people. Even if these problems are resolved as desired, what benefit will it bring to the elimination of the national crisis?

Negotiations for the Sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway

Russian and Puppet Claims Differ Greatly

Puppet Organization Demands Purchase at a Discounted Price

Soviet Russia Demands Security for the Maritime Province

(Tokyo) Regarding the issue of the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway, the claims of Japan, Russia, and Manchukuo are becoming clear, and the valuations of Japan and Russia differ greatly. According to the Toyo Keizai Shinpo, the claims of the puppet state, i.e., Japan, are as follows:

(1) The Chinese Eastern Railway has a very wide gauge, five feet, which is inconvenient for direct traffic with the South Manchurian Railway. In the future, it should be changed to a four-foot, eight-inch gauge, which will require huge expenses.

(2) The 400 million rubles of construction costs proposed by the Russian side include urban construction costs and school operating costs, which should be deducted.

(3) The line has been severely dilapidated recently and has undergone major repairs in the past, making it unusable. Currently, the monthly deficit reaches two to three million rubles.

(4) The puppet state plans to build parallel lines and longitudinal lines, which have little economic value.

(5) Since the Japanese army entered northern Manchuria, all real power has been in the hands of the Kwantung Army, which has lost its aggressive nature from the time of Imperial Russia.

Japan and Manchukuo are unwilling to pay a fair price based on the above reasons, while the Russian side claims as follows:

(1) Russia's sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway not only sells the railway but also completely withdraws all economic power from it. Therefore, it cannot be valued solely based on the Chinese Eastern Railway itself.

(2) Russia has voluntarily withdrawn from northern Manchuria, and Japan and Manchukuo should also stop their aggression against northern Sakhalin and the Maritime Province from now on. (3) The Chinese Eastern Railway is able to sustain itself in the environment of the world's economic crisis. The current losses are due to Japanese military actions and should not be used as a reason to reduce its valuation. (30th, China United Press)

(Moscow) The Communist Party newspaper Izvestia stated in an editorial today that the negotiations for the sale of the Chinese Eastern Railway will reveal whether Japan has sincere intentions for peace in the Far East. It also refuted the claim that this incident exposed Soviet Russia's weakness, saying that the Russian government has no political interests in Manchuria, only economic interests, which are based on the railway itself. It also said that Soviet Russia is unwilling to be drawn into the competition for spheres of influence, which is not in line with Soviet Russia's foreign policy. It then refuted the reports in Japanese newspapers that Russia will sell Vladivostok and eastern Siberia, calling them laughable rumors. It said that the Japanese are spreading rumors in order to reduce the 800 million Japanese yen that Soviet Russia is asking for the Chinese Eastern Railway, which the Russian people naturally do not find worth laughing at. (30th, National News Agency)

A Certain Diplomat Discusses the Conclusion of an Arbitration Treaty Between Japan and the United States

Unilateral Propaganda by the Japanese Side

(Nanjing) Although the US official has denied the conclusion of an arbitration treaty between Japan and the United States, the Japanese side is still conducting negotiations for propaganda. For this reason, a reporter from the Central News Agency specially visited a certain diplomat to inquire about his observations. According to the interview, Japan's foreign policy has changed significantly since its withdrawal from the League of Nations. Before Japan withdrew from the League of Nations, on the one hand, the United States repeatedly stated that it would not recognize the results of aggression, and on the other hand, there was a historical alliance between Britain and Japan. Therefore, Japan's foreign policy at this time was to unite with Britain and contain the United States. After withdrawing from the League of Nations, due to the Indian tariff issue, a serious economic conflict arose between Britain and Japan. The anti-British sentiment in Japan became increasingly fierce. Even in the World Economic Conference, it revealed an attitude of attacking Britain. It can be seen that the ill feelings between Britain and Japan are deepening day by day and will develop from economic conflicts to political conflicts. In order to avoid isolation from the League of Nations, the Japanese side shifted its focus and adopted a policy of uniting with the United States and containing Britain. However, the United States' foreign policy is not only traditionally consistent but also tends to shift from the Monroe Doctrine to a more active approach. Although the Japanese side has tried its best to coordinate and attempt to conclude an arbitration treaty, Japan's diplomacy, which has always lacked credibility, will certainly fail to win the trust of the United States. Judging from the repeated denials by American officials, it can be seen that the Japanese propaganda is entirely one-sided. (30th, Central News Agency)

Austrian Prime Minister, Undaunted by Violence, Strictly Prohibits Hitler's Party

Reuter, Vienna, 29th - Austrian Prime Minister Dr. Dollfuss arrived today in Innsbruck, the stronghold of the Austrian National Socialist Party. 15,000 people gave him a warm welcome. The authorities had made special preparations to prevent assassination attempts. The number of auxiliary police patrols along the route has been doubled. Train and car passengers are subjected to strict inspections. At noon, the bishop prayed for Dr. Dollfuss, and the people recited the prayers in unison. Dr. Dollfuss gave a speech to the crowd, reaffirming his determination not to be intimidated, and said that the responsibility of the Austrians is to be loyal to the motherland, regardless of party affiliation. He also said that the authorities had previously been very tolerant of the Austrian Social Party, but this had been seen as weakness, so the government will now act in accordance with the circumstances.

Change of Economic Ministers in the German Government

Brüning Considers Hitler's Words

Reuter, Berlin, 29th - Today, President Hindenburg accepted the resignation of Economic Minister Hugenberg and appointed Schmitt as Economic Minister and Darre as Food Minister. Hugenberg's resignation was triggered by the German government's ban on the National Rights Party. According to yesterday's government declaration, members of the National Rights Party will receive equal treatment with members of the National Socialist Party, and will be regarded as soldiers of the state and not discriminated against. Those who have been arrested will be released. Members of the National Rights Party in parliament and the federal council will join the National Socialist Party. The Catholic Party expects the government to take action against them soon. Former Prime Minister Brüning and other party leaders are currently considering Hitler's recent remarks. Catholic Party members in Berlin and Cologne have voluntarily dissolved today and are now requesting to join the National Socialist Party. The Bavarian state government has ordered the seizure of funds and properties of eight Catholic organizations, including those within Catholic territory. At the same time, the Prussian International Bible Research Association was dissolved for conspiring against the church and harboring communists. Today, the authorities announced that four senior members of the National Socialist Party have been arrested for attempting to undermine Hitler's proposals. It is reported that the four were previously captains in the army and intend to incite chambers of commerce to resist Hitler's decisions on economic issues.

Water Level of North Shandong Canal Rises

The Yellow River Remains Calm

Jinan Correspondence: Due to continuous heavy rain, the water level of the North Shandong Canal has continued to rise. The Construction Department received a long-distance phone call today from Sun Chaiyun, a technician stationed in Wucheng, reporting that the water level of the canal within Wucheng has reached 29.8 meters, and the situation is critical. After supervising the staff to work hard to protect it, it was fortunate that no danger occurred. In the afternoon, the water level dropped by two centimeters. Subsequently, a long-distance phone call was received from Sun Weihan, a technician stationed in Linqing, reporting that the canal's water level continued to rise, reaching 33.01 meters today. The highest water level in Linqing last autumn was only 34 feet. Now, before the major flood season, it is not much different from the highest water level, which is a rare phenomenon in recent years. Based on this, the Construction Department has telegraphed the magistrates of the six counties along the river—Linqing, Wucheng, De County, Guantao, Xiajin, and En County—and the technical personnel stationed in the county by the department to work hard to protect the area and not be negligent.

It is also reported that after the Yellow River in Zhengzhou rose by three feet, the provincial river affairs bureau immediately telegraphed the heads of all sections along the river to pay close attention. As of today, the water level has not risen significantly, and the working conditions are stable. The water level is around 28 meters, which is still three feet lower than the highest water level in the 20th year. Zhang Lianjia, Director of the River Affairs Bureau, said that although the current Yellow River water level is not low, it is still far from the danger line. The bureau has ordered all river workers to pay attention to protection, but also not to overreact, falsely report the water level, and shake people's hearts. The spring maintenance project this year was very good, and there has not been any unexpected major flood. It is possible that there will be no worries. Over a thousand sections of stone dikes have been completed along the entire river. Currently, stone materials are being purchased and transported to continue the repair. If the entire river is replaced with stone dikes, the Yellow River will surely reduce the risk of breaching in the future. (29th)

Disastrous Flooding in Hunan Province

=The Xiang, Zi, Yuan, and Li Rivers all Flood at Different Times=

Disaster Spreads, Counties Report Disaster

Changsha Correspondence: Since the beginning of summer, continuous rain has not stopped. In the upper reaches of western and southern Hunan, mountain floods have erupted, and the accumulated water has not receded. At the same time, the Yuan, Li, Xiang, and Zi Rivers have risen sharply, with floods overflowing and spreading, creating a disaster. More than 30 counties have reported major flooding. Although the sky has cleared in recent days, mountain floods continue to erupt unabated, and the water level has not decreased slightly. In addition, the water level of the Yangtze River has increased, and the water of the Xiang and Yuan Rivers cannot be discharged, causing the Yangtze River to backflow into the lake. As a result, the counties along the lake have suffered particularly heavy losses. The provincial government, the Department of Civil Affairs, and the Relief Committee have dispatched special commissioners to separately expedite the inspection of dikes, supervise flood control, and prepare for relief efforts. However, the water level continues to rise, and the disaster is expanding daily, which is very worrying. The following is a summary of the disaster reports from various counties in recent days.

Changde Dikes and Embankments Collapse

Zhou Shuzi, the Supervisor of Changde and Han, telegraphed the province, reporting: "Due to continuous heavy rain in Changde recently, the river water has risen sharply, more than two feet higher than the water level in the 20th year of the Republic. All of the Gu, Guanzi, Hucheng, Shanghucheng, Xialucheng, Xibaocheng, Dongbaocheng, Xilaixing, Xingfa, Tongxing, Fuxing, Yonggu, Jiu'an, Huzhu, Liuxi, Wan'an, Tangjiang, Wuyi, Gaofu, Hexing, Gong, Fu, Qiang, Fu, Zeng, Sanxing, Wufu, Shanjuan, Quan Zhangcici Dang, Zhongxing, Yilu, Tongle, Renyi, Xieji, Shengjia, Wu Huang, Ludi, Jiadi, Fuxing, Zhou Yaojia, and Xuxing embankments have successively collapsed. The rest are still being investigated and reported. Houses have been washed away, which is extremely tragic. I respectfully request that urgent relief be issued quickly to save the disaster-stricken people. Zhou Shuzi, Supervisor of Changde and Han, kowtows."

Taoyuan Highway Completely Submerged

The magistrate of Taoyuan County reported, "Since the 14th, heavy rain has continued, and mountain floods have erupted. The banks of the Yuan River and the areas of Qishi and Wuxi are all under water. The fields and houses are covered in mud. The Changtao Highway is completely submerged. The weather is still overcast, and the water continues to rise. All disaster reports will be submitted later after investigation. I respectfully report this by telegram for your review. Magistrate Liu Duanlian of Taoyuan County kowtows."

Yueyang Embankments Submerged

The magistrate of Yueyang County reported, "According to Hou Yuankun, a staff member of this government, who inspected the water situation in the eighth and ninth districts, he reported back to the county that due to continuous rain in recent days, the lake water has flooded, and all the sluice gates of the embankments have been closed. The lake water is higher than the embankment fields, and the accumulated water cannot be discharged. About 60% of the embankment fields have been submerged by the water. If the rain continues, the embankments will become a swamp. Although the embankment works are solid, if the lake water rises another three or four feet, there is a risk of collapse. I have ordered the district chiefs and embankment leaders to take strict precautions and report at any time. I respectfully report this by telegram for your review. Magistrate Hou Houzong of Yueyang County presents this report."

Yiyang Two Embankments Collapse

The magistrate of Yiyang County reported, "The subordinate county is located in the lower reaches of the Zi River, bordering the lake. The districts in the lower township are all embankment fields. Since the beginning of summer, the weather has been overcast and cold, with continuous rain for weeks. The Zi River has flooded several times. The Tongyou Embankment and Dongbai Embankment in the county's second district have both reported disasters due to water accumulation, and the rice seedlings have been submerged. Qianjiazhou, Yanjiabao Embankment, Yiyuan 16 Embankment, and others in the seventh district have also suffered disasters due to water accumulation. The Yongxing and Liang Embankments collapsed at 4 a.m. on the 16th of this month. In addition to dispatching personnel to investigate, I have also ordered the district chiefs to supervise the embankment leaders to prepare for defense and expedite rescue efforts. I have also dispatched capable political police to various embankments to suppress and assist, doing my best to protect them. Although the Zi River has receded slightly, the Yuan and Li Rivers have flooded at the same time, and the various embankments are still at risk. I hereby report the collapse of the embankments and the protection of the water situation by telegram. Magistrate Li Yu of Yiyang County kowtows."

Li County Water Rises Several Zhang

The magistrate of Li County reported, "In the past month, heavy rains have continued, and the embankments in the county have suffered internal collapses. On the days of Hanqiao, there were two mountain floods, and the water rose several zhang, endangering the county seat. More than ten embankments have collapsed, and people, livestock, and property have been washed away, which is extremely tragic. In addition to submitting a detailed report, I first report this by telegram. Magistrate Gui Tang of Li County and Director Wen Yun of the Provincial Tax Bureau kowtow." Another telegram said, "The telegram respectfully awaits your review. According to reports, Mengjiang Embankment and 35 other embankments collapsed on the evening of Hanqiao. I request that you continue to send personnel to investigate and distribute relief to save the disaster-stricken people. Magistrate Gui Tang of Li County kowtows."

Hengyang Disaster is Severe

The Civil Affairs Department previously sent Inspector Zhang Zugao to investigate the flood disaster in Heng County. According to yesterday's report, the disaster is very severe. The report is as follows: (1) The disaster area totals 935 square kilometers. (2) The current number of disaster victims is 34,829. (3) The situation of the disaster victims: 674 people are displaced. Most of the fields and gardens are submerged, and houses are washed away. They are living in temples and begging for food in other places, which is very miserable. (4) The death toll is 91, and more than 400 people were injured by collapsing fields and houses. (5) The loss of houses and property totals 1,269,000 silver dollars, including 842 houses and 406 shops. In addition, clothing, grain, rice, livestock, bridges, roads, and dams are estimated at 256,000 silver dollars. (6) More than 46,100 mu of fields have been submerged, of which more than 33,000 mu have suffered 50% damage, and more than 13,000 mu have been completely unproductive. In addition, more than 1,140 mu have been washed into channels or accumulated with sand and gravel like mountains, making them impossible to cultivate.

Liuyang Corpses Float By

Mountain floods erupted in Liuyang, and the city and countryside suffered severe flooding. Yin Zhongcai, the magistrate of the county, has reported this to the province. The Langli River in Changsha flows through Liuyang. On the 18th, the corps commander of the city reported to the city that more than a dozen male and female corpses had floated in the river in recent days. Furthermore, a dead woman was seen holding the corpse of her baby, only a few months old, in her arms, not letting go. It can be seen that the water came suddenly, and there was no time to escape. The corpses that have floated in have been buried by the local authorities. In addition, an old Wujiang boat was moored on the riverbank in the city. There were five men and women on board. Due to the surge of the Liuyang River flood, it was suddenly overturned. It was late at night, and the entire boat capsized, burying everyone in the fish's belly, which is truly tragic.

Xinhua Mine Shafts Submerged

A Xinhua mine owner reported that continuous heavy rain has caused disasters. Where water has accumulated, the low-lying mine shafts have become swamps. On the first day of the month, heavy rain poured down, not stopping for three days and nights. Until the morning of the 3rd day, mountain floods erupted suddenly. The Tianbao, Qiu Ji, and Sanrui mines of the Gongfuli Company, and the Tianxifu mine of Zhifu Company were flooded, causing the dams to break and drowning more than a dozen workers. Other mines, such as Kai Zhen, Tong Xin, Yong Fu, Qiu Fu, Chu Defu, Xie Ji, Fu He, Chang Yi, Fu Chou, Fu Tang, Fu He, Yu Tong, Fu Da, Sheng Lu, Xiang Ji, Yi Ji, and others in the Changlongjie Taotang Fanshan area, and Sanyu Sisi, Sheng Hou, Da Da Qing, Li Yuan, Da Dao, Jiu Pin, Gong Mei, Li Xing, Zhi He, Mei Li Yan, San You Tang, Yi Li, Fu Heng, Yi Li Yuan, Mei Li Yi, Bao Xing, Shi Fu, Bao Hou, San Yi, and San Mao Hao, Tie Ji, and others in the Tuzi Shu Oujia Chong area, as well as the Kaiyuan Company and other places in Feishuiyan, were all flooded and unable to work. The total loss is estimated to be over 100,000 yuan. Thousands of workers have lost their jobs. The disaster of being drowned is especially tragic. The weather is still not clearing. In addition to ordering the affected companies to add water equipment, strengthen flood prevention, and find ways to provide relief to unemployed workers, I hereby report the disaster by telegram for your review. I respectfully request prompt relief and await your orders. Town Director Yang Tonggeng of the Xinhua Mine Mountain Directly Subordinate Town Office, Chairman Wang Zicai of the Xinhua Antimony Industry Association, and Chairman Yang Zhiduan of the Xinhua Tin Mine Mountain Antimony Mine Industry Workers' Union kowtow.

Wuxi

Robbery and Assault in Shangyu Lane

Xia Ailin, a 48-year-old resident of Shangyu Lane in the fourth district (Kaiyuan Township) of the county, is a stone paving worker by profession. He has some savings and has two young sons. At around 10 p.m. on the night of the 29th, seven bandits came, wearing short blue cloth shirts and pants, and carrying two pistols. Four bandits climbed over the roof from the low houses next door and entered the courtyard, opening the gate. Three bandits were on guard outside, and set off firecrackers to show their power. After entering the room, the bandits shone flashlights and crowded upstairs, dragging Xia Ailin and his wife from the bed and forcing them to reveal the location of the hidden silver. Xia's wife replied that it was too late, and was hit with a wooden stick by the bandits. They then searched separately and robbed more than 90 silver dollars and about 100 copper coins from the bed. They also robbed a gold ring, two gold bracelets, three silver rings, and leather clothing, for a total loss of more than 200 yuan. After the bandits obtained the loot, they divided it in Qingshan Bay, leaving behind a clothing bag containing shrouds and other items. The next day, it was picked up by the villagers and returned to Xia's family. Liu Chunlan, the director of the 9th branch of the public security bureau in charge, immediately sent Patrol Chief Feng to lead the police to investigate and investigate the location where the bandits divided the spoils. On one hand, the victim Xia Ailin issued a loss report and reported to the public security bureau to request the arrest of the stolen goods.

Gold Lion and Jade Inkstone Discovered in Tianzhong

Dan A'genhe, a farmer in Qian Chen Lane, Baitu Township, Second District (i.e., Wang Aisheng), is over 30 years old and has three children. However, his family is destitute. This spring, through Wang Agui, he rented a mu of rice field from Zhao Qiu, a Chinese medicine practitioner in Baituqiao, for cultivation. A'genhe had already harvested the wheat in the field and was preparing to irrigate the water for rice planting. Suddenly, he discovered two urn heads in the mud in the eastern corner of the field, containing a gold lion, an jade inkstone, and two gold bars weighing more than 17 taels in total. In addition, there were 16 silver ingots with a wire plate style, each weighing five taels. A'genhe was overjoyed and put them on the table at home for the family to worship. Neighboring villagers who heard the news went to see them, and the road became blocked. Now, a jade shop in Suzhou is willing to pay 3,500 yuan to buy the gold lion and jade inkstone. A'genhe believes that the rare goods can be sold at a high price, so he has not yet sold them.

Yesterday (30th), at 4 p.m., two bandits dressed in blue and black trousers suddenly came to No. 7 Hetou, Xiaorihui Bridge South, outside Xumen, and robbed 141.6 yuan of big money, and injured the legs of women Wu Shenshi and Zhu Qianshi with gunshots before escaping with the loot.

Flight School Captain Falls and Dies

Chen Huifu, the captain of the cover team of the Central Aviation School in Jianqiao, Hangzhou, took a car to Qiaosi on official business a few days ago. Because the truck he was sitting in was bumping, he fell, causing serious head injuries to Captain Chen. Blood flowed like a fountain, and he was immediately sent to Guangji Hospital for treatment. He died at 8 a.m. yesterday morning. The school notified Captain Chen's family from his native place (Haining) to come to Hangzhou to take care of the funeral. All the students and officers of the school mourned him.

Tragic Murder of a Farmhand Occurs in West Lake

Qi Zhongbao, a 69-year-old farmer from Caoshe No. 6, Kuoshi Banqiao, West Lake, Hangzhou, is a native of the mountains and usually grows vegetables there. His wife, Qi Xushi, is 54 years old. He has a son and a daughter. Yu A'mao, who is 30 years old, also farms at home. The daughter, Xu Qishi, who is 27 years old, is somewhat attractive. She married Xu Kaitai, a gardener, and lives at No. 11 Renhe Road, Hangzhou City. Because her mother's house is close by, she often goes home. In the 17th year of the Republic, she had an affair with Monk Xinkong, who used to live in the Golden Cave and now lives in the Liutong Temple. On the tenth day of the fourth month of the lunar calendar, Xu Qishi and Xinkong were having illicit relations when they were seen by the farmhand Shen A'fa. Qi Zhongbao was afraid of being exposed, which would affect his face, so he struck first and tragically killed Shen A'fa with a kitchen knife, stabbing him thirteen times and killing him. At about 9 p.m. that night, Qi and another short-term worker, Qi Demao, carried the corpse to the foot of the vegetable garden wall opposite and buried it to cover up the traces. On the afternoon of the 29th, Qi Demao was discussing the report with his fellow villagers in a teahouse in the bustling city when he was overheard by a bystander, who immediately reported it to Patrol Chief Chen Peijin of the sixth sub-bureau of the second district, who went to find Qi Demao. After detailed questioning, Qi revealed everything. Inspector Sun Hengji was sent to lead Demao to identify the burial site at night, and the corpse was found buried there. The police immediately arrested Qi Zhongbao and others and confiscated the murder weapon. Xinkong was also arrested. The confessions of the criminals were evasive, and they claimed that they were arguing with Qi Demao and were killed. However, Qi Xushi has admitted that the deceased was killed by her husband. The main culprit could not deny it. At 1 p.m. yesterday (30th), the Hangzhou Local Court sent Prosecutor Chen Huaming and Clerk Feng Shengxiang to examine the body, and it was confirmed that there were thirteen knife wounds on the throat, causing death. The corpse was moved to the Qingbomen Cemetery in a coffin. The six murderers were handed over to the Public Security Bureau to be transferred to the court for trial.

Special Issue on Cooperative Movement

The Way Out for China's Cooperative Movement by Wu Juenong

What is the goal of the cooperative movement? Thirty years ago, Dr. Hans Hullor made it clear at the Sixth International Cooperative Alliance Congress: "This is a movement for us to strive for independence and freedom in our economic and social living conditions." Although it was opposed at the time by a small group of those who believed in Christian-style "You must love your neighbor," his judgment has become increasingly meaningful and powerful as time goes on!

Since 1844, about ninety years ago, when the Rochdale Pioneers Cooperative Society in England was established, cooperative societies now exist almost everywhere humans live, and the number of people worldwide who have joined cooperative societies accounts for more than one-fifth of the total population. Indeed, because it is a movement that peacefully strives for economic and social independence and freedom, it does not provoke strong opposition from capitalism.

However, despite this, while we see the cooperative movement developing in this way, on the other hand, various countries differ in their circumstances, content, and methods. Consumer cooperative societies in England have special prosperity, credit cooperative societies have meaningful development in Germany, France focuses on production cooperation, Belgium develops insurance cooperation, and Denmark focuses on sales cooperation for milk and eggs. These are still formal distinctions, the most different being that the development of the cooperative movement in Europe is from the bottom up, in other words, it is an organization automatically formed by the people. In the East, such as Japan and India, most are from the top down, that is, the government makes every effort to promote and guide them. Furthermore, Russia uses the methods of the cooperative movement to complete its socialist foundation, while Belgium uses it as a weapon of the Socialist Party. Pan-Germanists in Italy and recently in Germany are even using coercion and enticement to try to make cooperative organizations part of their operational structure. Therefore, although the cooperative movement permeates the entire world, its methods vary; although cooperativists argue vehemently over various theories, in reality, they have long established their own separate approaches based on the political organization and social environment of each country.

China's cooperative movement has only a little over ten years of history, its foundation is extremely weak, and its achievements are naturally very immature. In recent years, due to the impending bankruptcy of rural villages and considerable promotion by the government, it seems to have made some progress, but the cooperative movements in various countries arise with the development of capitalism. China's national capital is still very weak, and urban financial capital is also abnormally and temporarily concentrated in cities due to the current unrest in the interior. In other words, China's current situation is completely under the control of imperialist financial capitalists, and the so-called domestic financial capital is merely an appendage of international capitalism. Therefore, China's cooperative movement definitely cannot arbitrarily copy and agree with the practices of other countries. This is an undeniable fact.

Let's take a few facts as examples. Recently, most cooperative comrades have said that there is no hope for the development of consumer cooperation in China, and that attention should be paid to agricultural cooperation in the future. Why can't consumer cooperation develop in China? The fact is that the majority of China's population are farmers. They wear simple clothes and eat coarse food, and are originally in a state of self-sufficiency, but now, after decades of exploitation by imperialists and feudal toxins, they are all in a state of semi-starvation, and there is almost no so-called consumption to speak of. Consumers are only residents in cities. A portion of city residents are non-productive consumers, they have free time and surplus cash, and they "don't care" about buying expensive goods. Moreover, there are various tax-evading and smuggling goods in cities, and there are bargain sales of cheap goods from various countries. With low prices and good quality, there is naturally no need to organize consumer cooperative societies. Others are non-resident employees, small merchants, vagrants, and workers. Firstly, they lack the ideology of anti-capitalism and anti-imperialism; secondly, they also lack the concept of unity and savings; and thirdly, and more importantly, they are accustomed to living under a feudal social organization, relying entirely on buying and selling on credit to eke out their years. Therefore, the simplest slogans of consumer cooperation: "Consumption is savings" and "Purchase must be in cash" are ultimately incompatible.

But is there hope for agricultural cooperation? If we cannot identify goals and establish a comprehensive plan, I predict that there will be no good results.

The most important and original organization of agricultural cooperation is credit cooperation. The first goal of credit cooperation is the self-savings of members, and the second is to borrow money from outside the society based on the credit of the entire society. China's farmers are already so poor that most of them are in debt. How can we talk about savings? As for borrowing money from outside the society, high-interest loans are of course excluded, and at present, rural banks and loan offices in various places not only have weak funds and difficult distribution, but also the interest of about one percent and short-term loans of half a year to a year, will they truly remedy the farmers' situation? I'm afraid no one can give me a satisfactory answer. Although recent financial capital has intentions to invest in rural areas, whether it has the strength has become a question, and whether it can truly benefit the farmers has become an important question for those who discuss the rural economy.

Let's talk about production and sales cooperation: The current commercial organization is extremely complex. If farmers can cooperate and sell directly on their own, they can naturally eliminate the profits of some small merchants, but the final handling institutions are still in the hands of foreign merchants and large factories in big cities. If their exploitative relationship is not eliminated, there is no hope of profiting from the trade of agricultural products. In recent years, the large-scale imports of rice, wheat, and cotton have left producers in the interior with no hope of survival, and what's more, the prices of all agricultural products are originally below the necessary production costs. Recently, cooperativists in various countries have been striving to directly link production cooperation with consumer cooperation, the purpose of which is to do just this, and since China's consumer cooperation is so immature and has so little hope, the lack of hope for production cooperation and even production and sales cooperation is also conceivable.

So, how should China's cooperative movement seek a path to survival? Here, limited by space, let's briefly list a few outlines:

First, the government should use all its strength. For example, in terms of finance, there must be at least three to five hundred million in working capital to provide loans to credit cooperative societies at the lowest interest rate. Second, regarding all production, sales, and farmers' distribution and consumption, it should be under the control of the government and be the organization for all activities. Third, the goal of organizing various cooperative societies is not only economic transformation, but must also bear the responsibility of social transformation, internally to eliminate all feudal forces, and externally to resist international imperialism. Fourth, this cooperative organization will naturally be from the top down, and should also have a degree of compulsion.

This was originally not my personal observation. Last year, many cooperative experts from the China Cooperative Society had such important resolutions in their plans to prosper rural areas through cooperative methods. Now, taking advantage of the opportunity of holding a cooperative propaganda movement, I will further elaborate on it.

One of the Most Important Pages in the History of the Cooperative Movement

The annual meeting of the China Cooperative Society in October of last year passed the "Plan to Prosper Rural Areas Through Cooperative Methods. This is one of the most important pages in the history of the Chinese Cooperative Movement." The article is tens of thousands of words long, and due to space limitations, it cannot be published in its entirety. Only an outline of the plan is recorded here to give a glimpse of the whole picture. Readers who want to see the whole picture should consult the report of the Third General Meeting of Members of the Society.

Two. Organization

(1) Establish cooperative authorities in the central government and various provinces and cities.

(2) Governments at all levels shall organize various cooperative societies and cooperative federations at all levels for farmers across the country within a time limit.

Three. Implementation

(1) Establish farmers' financial institutions in the central government and various provinces, cities, counties, and districts.

(2) Find ways to effectively connect consumer cooperative societies with production cooperative societies.

(3) The central government shall find ways to encourage and support the organization of land use cooperative societies.

(4) Agricultural research institutions shall take cooperative methods as the goal of their implementation.

(5) Establish a cooperative training institute.

(6) The assessment of administrative personnel shall include matters related to handling cooperation.

(7) Connect party and government agencies and cooperative technical groups to jointly study various issues related to cooperative administrative undertakings.

Four. Guidance

(1) Party departments at all levels across the country shall uniformly mobilize for cooperative undertakings.

(2) All schools across the country shall implement various cooperative undertakings.

(3) In cooperative laws and regulations, various awards and preferential treatments shall be compiled. (End)

Recent European Cooperative Movement by Peng Shiqin

For this International Cooperative Movement Propaganda Week, the editor assigned me this topic because I had just returned from Europe to study cooperative undertakings. Due to space and time constraints, I can only give a general overview.

The trends of the European cooperative movement, to name a few major ones, are roughly as follows:

(1) Integration and unification. The establishment of European cooperative societies is all from the bottom up. The poor classes, due to practical needs, unite people in similar circumstances and organize a cooperative society. At the beginning of their establishment, the scale was very small. For example, consumer cooperative societies are only for eliminating the exploitation of retail merchants and grocery stores. This was still able to deal with the enemy in the early days of the cooperative movement. By the end of the nineteenth century, the situation had changed greatly. These small-scale cooperative societies gradually felt that it was not easy to survive. After the war, due to the progress of commercial organizations, it was even more precarious. To save themselves, they had to unite and increase their own strength. Thus, the idea of ​​mergers spread throughout Europe. At this time, it was only the integration of small cooperative societies with the same purpose in the same region, which was a defensive front. Recently, those in charge of cooperative central organizations in various countries have wanted to unite cooperative societies of the same nature in one country under a consistent system from top to bottom, as a prerequisite for the second to fourth items to be discussed below, to prepare to counterattack the enemy and transform the lineup.

The work of integration is still in progress today. Looking at recent statistics, whether it is consumer cooperative societies, production cooperative societies, or credit cooperative societies, especially German agricultural credit cooperative societies, although the number of newly established societies is more than the number of bankrupt societies, the total number is often slightly less than in previous years. This is precisely the result of integration. As for unification, it is more difficult to achieve than integration. This is not only affected by the religious or political colors of cooperative societies, but also by the stubbornness of a group of founders. We have already seen that cooperative societies are very small in scale at the beginning of their establishment. However, if they are managed properly and have a long history, they can often develop to a considerable important position. The founders of these cooperative societies that have reached a considerable important position often pride themselves on this and are unwilling to make themselves subordinate to others. It is possible to join a wholesale cooperative society as a member, but they are ultimately unwilling to sacrifice their independent facade. This phenomenon is still easy to encounter in Belgium, but it is gradually getting better.

(2) Link between production cooperation and consumer cooperation. Before consumer cooperative societies expand to their own production, all consumer goods must be purchased from abroad: either from capitalist producers or from production cooperative societies. However, whether it is from the former or the latter, conflicts of interest between each consumer society and the price are inevitable. Let's not mention capitalist producers for the time being; Professor Gide has described the relationship between production cooperative societies and consumer cooperative societies very accurately in one of his books. Although production cooperative societies are not for profit, they only take back the part that is devoured by middlemen, because they believe that this is the part of their products that is exploited. However, consumer cooperative societies believe that this is the part that is exploited when they purchase, and they also demand to take back the whole part. Therefore, when these two types of cooperative societies trade, they do not give way to each other, so that they cannot get close. At the same time, capitalist producers and middlemen reap the benefits. Recently, both sides have realized that this phenomenon is a major obstacle to the future of the cooperative movement. If so, the saying that consumer cooperative societies and production cooperative societies, especially consumer cooperative societies and agricultural cooperative societies, should be linked has become increasingly popular. National cooperative congresses and the International Cooperative Alliance in various countries all recognize this as a major current issue. Before the emergence of the cooperative republic and before the abolition of the wage system, this relationship is to organize the economy nationally and internationally under conditions that meet needs. Moreover, the need for consumer cooperative societies and agricultural cooperative societies to be linked is especially emphasized by the promoters of the cooperative movement in various countries. Because agricultural cooperative societies directly operated by farmers are often better in terms of technology and production than agricultural cooperative societies operated by urban consumers. Therefore, in recent years, there have been increasing reports of consumer cooperative societies and agricultural cooperative societies establishing letters of understanding and transaction contracts. Moreover, consumers have incorporated the established agricultural production organizations into agricultural cooperative societies, eliminating the past competition and jealousy. The consumer cooperative in Geneva, Switzerland, abandoned its own milk business and is entirely supplied by the Geneva Milk Cooperative, which is a clear example.

(3) Progress of wholesale cooperation. Under the concentrated phenomenon of modern capitalism, the elimination of small enterprises by large enterprises is a natural result. This is especially evident in industry and commerce. The reason why small handicraftsmen can still survive is that artistic products cannot be made by machines. The reason why retailers can still maintain themselves is that the credit system is not popular in capitalist large stores on the one hand, and is not allowed by cooperative principles on the other hand. At the current stage, since cooperative societies are unable to produce on their own and directly supply wholesale cooperative societies, the application of wholesale cooperation is not only the only way to reduce the cost of purchasing goods, but also an important condition for being able to maintain themselves undefeated against all private businesses. Although this principle has long been worked hard for by cooperativists, it has not been fully realized according to the planned plan due to various reasons. In some countries, they are still in the era of simple wholesale places, without warehouse equipment, and only representatives of secondary cooperative societies from various places gather at the wholesale place once a week to collect order documents and transfer them to suppliers to directly ship to various places. (To be continued) (This article solicits submissions for the Economics Special Issue of this newspaper next Monday)

Local News

Central Mint

New Currency Begins Circulation

After the Auditing Committee sealed it, it was sent to the Central Bank yesterday

Circulation in the market within four days due to the accounting period

The new currency minted by the Central Mint and announced by the Ministry of Finance to be issued today has been examined and approved by the Auditing Committee, proving that the new currency has been sent to the Central Bank for issuance yesterday, and the results of the examination have been announced. The details are as follows:

Car Sent to the Bank

After the establishment of the auditing office of the Auditing Committee Secretariat, it immediately conducted an examination in accordance with the regulations of the auditing charter. The new currency minted by the Central Mint with the new model is in line with the legal fineness and weight. From yesterday onwards, the Auditing Committee will put the qualified new currency into boxes of 5,000 dollars each, and affix the seal of the Auditing Committee on the four sides of the box. The certificate of the chairman and examiner in Chinese and Western languages ​​is affixed on the front, and a number is compiled. At 1:00 p.m., the Central Mint sent 3 million dollars of the new currency with certificates to the Central Bank for deposit.

Giving a Certificate

The original text of the certificate of conformity after the inspection is as follows: Certificate of the Auditing Committee of the Central Mint. For the matter of issuing a certificate, the Central Mint is approved to send a box of silver dollars, a total of 5,000 dollars, to the association for inspection in accordance with Article 6 of the auditing charter of this association. After inspection in accordance with Article 7 of the same charter, the fineness is in accordance with Article 2 of the Silver Standard Coinage Regulations. In accordance with Article 8 of the auditing charter, a certificate is issued. This certificate, Chairman Kong Xiangxi, Examiner Ge Lan De, July 1, 22nd year of the Republic of China.

Today's Report

Chief Engineer Ge Lan De examined the fineness batch by batch, extracting one dollar for every 10,000 dollars for examination. It is said that the result is that the fineness is excellent. As for his examination report, it was originally intended to be released yesterday afternoon, but it was changed to be released at noon today so that all sectors could understand the fineness of the new currency, so that it can be circulated smoothly.

Circulation on the 4th

Although the new currency examined and approved by the Central Mint is scheduled to be issued today, today is the end of the 22nd year of the banking industry's previous session. Acceptance is suspended. Banks on the Bund will not resume acceptance until July 4. Therefore, the circulation of new currency in the local market will have to wait until the banking industry resumes acceptance on the 4th.

Guerrilla Army Attacks Yingkou

Heavy Losses for the Japanese Army

Yingkou is an important port in the Northeast. A large amount of soybeans, soybean cakes, soybean oil, etc., are shipped every year. After the puppet state forcibly occupied the customs and arbitrarily increased tariffs, the South China gangs stopped handling goods to Yingkou completely. Business in the Niuzhuang area has declined to the extreme. This time, the "Tunan" ship of the China Merchants Bureau arrived in Yingkou, just in time for the guerrilla army to attack Yingkou. The details are as follows:

Guerrilla Army Attacks

The "Tunan" ship arrived in Yingkou on June 24, having sailed from Shanghai. On the day before the ship arrived in Yingkou, a large force of the guerrilla army attacked Yingkou again. The guerrillas' purpose was initially not to occupy Yingkou, but to inflict heavy damage on the Japanese army. When the guerrillas attacked to within 14 miles of Yingkou, the Yingkou market had already experienced extreme panic. The Japanese army hurriedly set off and fought with the guerrillas near Yingkou. As a result, five Japanese officers were killed and many soldiers were injured, while the guerrillas also withdrew.

Japanese Army Deaths

From the 24th onwards, the Japanese army declared martial law in Yingkou. Armed military police were stationed on the streets, and traffic was cut off at 8:00 p.m. Unless there were special symbols and passwords, passage was not allowed. The search of people from outside was even stricter, so that after sunset, there was no one on the streets. On the day the "Tunan" ship arrived in Yingkou, the Japanese army stationed in Yingkou held a memorial service for the five Japanese officers who had been killed by the guerrillas, and sent the bones of the deceased to Dalian for transportation back to Japan.

All Industries Depressed

Yingkou's major products, such as soybean cakes, oil, and miscellaneous grains, are mostly sold to Shantou, Xiamen, Guangdong, and other ports. Recently, due to the puppet state's increase in export taxes, the South China gangs have implemented a cessation of procurement. The special commissioners sent by Shantou, Xiamen, and Guangdong to handle goods have all withdrawn, and the silk and satin merchants and southern goods stores operated by Guangdong people in Yingkou are also closing down and returning south, causing the Yingkou market to be depressed in all industries. State-owned ships occasionally sail to Yingkou, mostly empty, and freight rates have fallen sharply. There is no cargo to carry. This time, the "Tunan" waited for many days, but only managed to load several thousand soybean cakes. At present, the Yingkou branch bureaus have all telegraphed to Shanghai, stating that business is in extreme decline and requesting that fewer ships be sent to avoid losses from empty voyages.

Navigation Measurement Bureau Notice: Riverboats Slow Down

Protect the Levee

The Navigation Measurement Bureau of the Navy Department, in view of the recent rise in river water, especially in the section from Jiujiang to Hankou, and in view of the possibility that the newly built levees on both sides of the river may not be strong and may collapse, specially issued a notice to the navigation industry yesterday that all large and small ships passing through low-lying areas along the river must slow down and stay away from the levees, so that they will not be destroyed by the torrents. This warning is intended to protect the lives and property of residents along the river, so all large and small ships must absolutely comply with it when sailing in that area.
