Shanghai Telephone Company in the Area of Cross-Border Road Construction

Automatic Telephone Installation Completed

Automatic Connection from Midnight Tonight

Company's Operating Report for Last Year

After the temporary resolution of the Shanghai Telephone Company's issue of cross-border road construction, it immediately replaced the telephones in the area of cross-border road construction in the northern district with fully automatic telephones. The project has now been completed and is scheduled to be fully converted to automatic connection from midnight tonight. According to the northern district's cross-border road construction area telephones, since the northern district automatic connection room was put into operation in February last year, all calls to that area have been automatically connected. However, outgoing calls still used manual connection, with operators dialing the listed numbers in the northern district connection room on behalf of the users. Now, it has been changed to automatic connection, completely the same as telephones in other areas. The company released its operating report and financial summary for last year, with total revenue of 3,500,450 taels for the entire year, an increase of 1,083,929 taels compared to the previous year. Various expenses, including depreciation, totaled 2,282,796 taels, an increase of 161,152 taels compared to the previous year. However, after deducting various interest charges, the company's operating loss was still 71,372 taels, which was less than the loss of 107,237 taels in the previous year. This loss was largely due to increased expenses during the period of converting to automatic telephones. As for the number of users, there were 44,606 at the end of last year, an increase of 6,177 compared to the end of the previous year, approximately 16 percent. Since the introduction of automatic telephones last autumn, the number of calls made by each user has increased rapidly. In the past year, the number of calls made per day has more than doubled compared to before. Therefore, although the telephone fee increased in March last year, the average cost per call for users has decreased by 24 percent compared to the time of manual connection.

Li Du's Representatives Go to Hong Kong Today to Welcome Li

General Li Du took the Italian postal ship "Conte Verde" on the 14th of last month to return to China, and is expected to pass through Hong Kong on the 6th and arrive in Shanghai on the 8th. General Li's representatives in Shanghai, Liu Piguang, Li's adjutant Wang Ziyao, and Counselor Jiang Ying, will take the "Sabrogan" ship to Hong Kong today to welcome General Li. Wang Ziyao was originally scheduled to fly to Xinjiang the day before yesterday to inspect the troops stationed in Xinjiang on behalf of General Li. However, because General Li's return to China was imminent, he decided to meet with General Li for instructions before setting off. Liu and Wang went to the Municipal Government yesterday to request protection when General Li arrives in Shanghai.

China-England Corporation Writes to Two Railway Bureaus

Regarding the Arrangement and Payment of Overdue Loan Interest

Railway Bureau Replies That It Saves 7,000 Yuan Monthly

According to the Xinsheng News Agency, the China-England Bank Corporation stated that the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administrations have repeatedly declared their inability to pay the principal and interest on overdue loans, while the railway lines have not increased, and the number of staff has increased year by year. Therefore, on the 15th of last month, it sent a letter to the heads of the two railway bureaus, urging them to consider the matter and restore the financial stability of the two railways to its previous level. The following is a record of the correspondence:

Letter of Request for Consideration

To Director Huang and Deputy Director Wu:

We are grateful to receive your letter of May 11, together with a copy of the first quarter work summary for the 22nd year of your bureau. Mr. Pousset has already read this report with great interest, and we understand that you consider the economy to be the lifeblood of the railway and regard it as the most important thing. This coincides with our own view. We also learned that your bureau has implemented frugality in stationery and materials, and has strictly restricted free tickets and benefit tickets, which is admirable. However, in general, it seems that your bureau's internal division of labor is in danger of being excessively detailed. Therefore, there are inevitably too many staff employed. This can be verified by looking at the number of staff in the Railway Statistics published by the Ministry of Railways. Although this did not start after you took office, it may be helpful to compare the number of staff over the years. The annual number of employees for both of your railways is as follows: 1916: 7,251; 1920: 8,564; 1923: 10,009; 1926: 10,639; 1929: 12,183; 1930: 12,505; 1931: 12,885; 1932: 13,071; 1933: 12,199.

From this, it can be seen that the rate of increase in your bureau's employees is very large. Although the railway business is said to be prospering year by year, the railway lines of your two railways have not increased. Although a connecting line was once added, after the connecting line was completed, your two railway bureaus merged into one and jointly managed the business, which in theory should have saved even more money. We sincerely hope that you will consider this issue and restore the financial stability of the two railways to its previous level. This is our earnest hope, and we look forward to seeing its realization. From a public point of view, it is generally believed that the railway's ability to repay its debts is a model of management performance. The Beijing-Shanghai Railway has repeatedly stated that it is unable to repay the overdue loans, and those who hold the bonds believe that the railway's reputation is now such that they are sending letters to newspapers to express their dissatisfaction. This shows the extent of public indignation. Now that the railway is fortunate to have you working hard to rectify it, it should be able to arrange for the payment of one installment of interest on the overdue debt in the shortest possible time, so that those who invested in the Chinese railway in the past can alleviate their anxiety. With this special letter, we offer our best wishes.

Sincerely,

Pousset

Railway Bureau's Explanation

To Mr. Pousset:

We are grateful to receive your letter of May 15, in which you mentioned that the number of employees on both railways has increased year by year, and that the principal and interest on the loans have been delayed for a long time, and urged us to consider the matter. Since we, Boqiao and others, have taken charge of the two railways, our only focus has been on economizing on unnecessary expenses, while focusing our efforts on productive undertakings. It is only when business increases that the principal and interest on the loans can be paid on time. As for the increase in personnel, it has been found that the five departments of the bureau—General Affairs, Engineering, Mechanical Affairs, Accounting, and Materials—have actually decreased rather than increased compared to last year. However, the Transportation Department has had to moderately add the lowest-level employees as assistants in order to handle responsible transportation. However, this was approved by the Ministry of Railways in advance, and was not initiated after Boqiao and others took office. In addition, the police department has added police officers because the police force on the two railways is weak, and it is necessary to add police officers at the time of responsible transportation. Most of the authority to employ people is controlled by the Railway Police Administration. Therefore, the number of people in the Transportation Department and the Police Department has slightly increased, but in terms of salaries, it has actually saved 7,092 yuan per month. We have enclosed a comparison table for your review. We hope that you will give us your advice from time to time so that we can correct our shortcomings. We are very grateful. We wish you good health.

Sincerely,

Huang Boqiao and Wu Shaozeng

Ma Zhanshan Returned to Shanghai from Beijing Yesterday Morning

Convening his Subordinates to Discuss Relief for Refugees and Officers

Receiving Reporters at 10:00 AM This Morning to Report on Everything

Various Organizations Held a Meeting Yesterday to Prepare a Grand Welcome

Generals Ma Zhanshan and Su Bingwen, the newly appointed members of the Military Affairs Commission, went to Beijing and then to Jiangxi from Shanghai to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to report on the anti-Japanese war and ask for instructions on everything. Now that they have completed their official duties, they returned from Jiangxi with their entourage of about a dozen people, taking the Jardine Matheson's De He steamer and the Taikoo Company's Wuhu steamer. They arrived in Beijing on the morning of the 28th. Mr. Ma and Mr. Su disembarked together, and Mr. Su immediately transferred to the early express train to Shanghai and Hangzhou to visit his wife and daughters. Mr. Ma took the train to Shanghai from Beijing on the afternoon of the 27th at 5:25 PM and arrived in port at 12:25 AM yesterday morning. His whereabouts were extremely secret, and he is scheduled to receive reporters at 10:00 AM this morning to report on all matters, which will be recorded as follows:

Very Few Knew

Generals Ma Zhanshan and Su Bingwen returned to the country in early June and went to Beijing and then to Jiangxi to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to report on the anti-Japanese war. They stayed in Nanchang for seven days and in Lushan for eleven days, and then, together with Lang Guanpu, the acting chairman of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government, and others, took the Jardine Matheson's De He steamer and the Taikoo Company's Wuhu steamer eastward. They arrived in Beijing on the morning of the 28th. Mr. Ma and Mr. Su disembarked together, and the rest of the entourage took the original steamer to Shanghai, arriving in port on the morning of the 27th. Mr. Su immediately transferred to the early express train to Shanghai and Hangzhou on the afternoon of the 27th to visit his wife and sons. General Ma arrived in Shanghai by train from Beijing at 12:25 AM yesterday morning. The matter was kept strictly confidential in advance. At that time, apart from Zhang Dianjiu, the deputy commander of the Northeastern People's National Salvation Army, and three or five others who remained in Shanghai, very few outsiders knew about it.

Visited General Zhu

After arriving in port, Mr. Ma went directly to his son Ma Kui's private residence in Sande Lane, Luban Road, to rest. However, because he was tired from the journey, he felt a slight headache and eye problems after arriving in port yesterday morning. He then went to a doctor's office with Deputy Commander Zhang Dianjiu for a consultation, and then went to visit General Zhu Ziqiao to discuss the placement of his subordinates. Mr. Ma is scheduled to receive the Shanghai press at the Huizhong Hotel on Sanma Road at 10:00 AM today (the 1st) to discuss everything in detail.

Discussing Relief

There are many Northeastern refugees who have returned to the country this time, most of whom are family members of those who died in battle. There are about 400 people in Beiping and about 200 in Shanghai. There are also about 200 family members of military officers, for a total of about 800 people. Some are stationed in Xinjiang, displaced and in dire straits. Representatives from Beiping also came to Shanghai yesterday to appeal for help. Mr. Ma immediately sent people to handle the matter. The various charitable organizations in Shanghai are maintaining their food and lodging, which is only a temporary measure. In order to seek fundamental relief, Mr. Ma specially invited Zhang Dianjiu, Lang Guanpu, and senior officials such as Liang Zhenduo and Xu Jingde yesterday morning to discuss ways to relieve the refugees.

Meeting Subordinates

Mr. Ma had planned to inspect the Jiangwan and Wusong war zones in Zhabei yesterday morning, but he was unable to do so due to the meeting. In the afternoon, his subordinates, including Zhang Dianjiu, the deputy commander of the Northeastern People's Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army, Xu Jingde, the commander of the Heihe garrison, Zhou Weitai, the director of the Heilongjiang Provincial Industry Department, Lang Guanpu, the director of the Finance Department, Wang Erzhan, the deputy commander of the Hulunbuir Railway Protection Army, Wu Delin, the commander of the Second Brigade, and Duan Zhongshang and Wu Huanzhang, Mr. Ma's representatives in Ping and Shanghai, were all received and interviewed by Mr. Ma. General Ma was unwell due to the fatigue of the journey and suffered from a severe headache. He plans to be hospitalized for treatment and recuperation within the next few days.

Personnel Arriving Together

Those who accompanied General Ma to Shanghai this time include Lang Guanpu, the director of the Heilongjiang Provincial Government's Finance Department, Zhou Weigong, the director of the Industry Department, Ke Yin, the secretary, Li Nongjun, Guo Zhushu, the director of the secretariat of the Su Department, and Deputy Adjutant Zhang, and more than a dozen others. They are currently staying at the Huizhong Hotel on Hankou Road.

Mr. Lang's Talk

Yesterday afternoon, the reporter visited Lang Guanpu at the Huizhong Hotel to inquire about everything. Mr. Lang replied that General Ma and others had completed their official duties in Jiangxi and took the Jardine Matheson's De He steamer eastward a few days ago. When the steamer arrived at Xiaguan, Mr. Ma and Deputy Adjutant Zhang disembarked and transferred to the Beijing-Shanghai United Transport to Shanghai. He (Mr. Lang) continued to take the original steamer and arrived in Shanghai the other day. When Mr. Ma came to Shanghai from Beijing this time, he was afraid that people from all walks of life in the city would come to welcome him, so he did not dare to bother them. Therefore, he did not telegraph in advance, so very few outsiders knew about it. Mr. Ma's most important task in leaving Jiangxi and sweeping Shanghai this time is to deal with the aftermath of his subordinates. Since Generals Ma and Su returned to the country, a total of about forty or fifty people from Mr. Ma's side and about seventy or eighty people from Mr. Su's side have come to Shanghai and are now staying in Shanghai waiting to be placed. As for the troops in Heilongjiang Province, they are currently led jointly by Division Commander Deng Wen, Independent Brigade Commander Li Haiqing, and Regiment Commander Tang. Mr. Ma plans to stay in Shanghai for a long time to recuperate.

Preparing a Welcome

The Shanghai Municipal Organizations' Preparatory Committee for Welcoming the Anti-Japanese Heroes Generals Ma and Su held a preparatory committee meeting at the committee's office at 2:00 PM yesterday. Those who attended the meeting included Shen Tianxin, Chen Yafu, Fang Difei, Sun Mingqi, Wang Jian'e, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, Ye Jiaxing, Liu Zhongying, Zheng Dongshan, Liang Gengshun, Zhang Chiseng, Ge Futian, and more than a dozen others. The meeting was chaired by Shen Tianxin. The following resolutions were passed: (1) Shen Tianxin and Wang Honghui were appointed to meet with General Ma Zhanshan in person; (2) A welcome meeting will be held on a fixed date after the meeting; (3) Another meeting will be held at 2:00 PM tomorrow afternoon to discuss the details. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Su Will Return to Shanghai Soon

General Su Bingwen previously sent Representative Fan Ruizheng to Shanghai to express his condolences to the families of the officers and soldiers who remained in Shanghai. Mr. Fan returned to Hangzhou yesterday to report back. According to Mr. Fan, General Su will come to Shanghai soon to take care of everything. As for the date of Commander Zhang Dianjiu's trip to the north, it is not yet certain. It is expected that it will be determined after meeting with General Su in Shanghai.

Standing Committee of Benevolent Organizations

The Joint Relief Association of Charitable Organizations for Northeastern Refugees received a telegram from Xu Shiying from Lushan, reporting on the meeting with Generals Ma and Su to discuss ways to relieve Northeastern refugees. Ma and Su agreed to join the association and go to Nanyang to raise relief funds. The association issued a notice yesterday, stating that a meeting will be held at the Renji Hall at 4:00 PM tomorrow to elect Ma and Su as standing committee members of the association. Xu's original telegram read: (Omissions) The report on Yangri's fundraising advertisement is extremely admirable. Your brother has been with Generals Ma Xiufang and Su Hanzhang in the mountains for days, and he knows that they are concerned about the Northeastern refugees and are willing to work with people from all walks of life to raise relief funds. At that time, I persuaded them to join the Standing Committee of this Association, and they all agreed. I also asked them to go to Nanyang to raise relief funds. The two generals are loyal, benevolent, and eager to help those in need. It is proposed that this association hold a special meeting to elect the two generals Ma and Su as standing committee members, which will definitely benefit the future of relief work. How can we expect a reply? Shiying bows, Qin.

Six Shipping Companies Suspend Sailings and Reduce Flights

To Be Implemented Starting Today

The Yangtze River shipping industry is in decline, and the various shipping companies have held meetings to implement austerity measures and reduce flights in order to minimize losses. The news was reported in yesterday's newspaper. The following is a continuation of the news:

Number of Ships of Six Major Companies

On the Yangtze River route, the six companies with the largest business in Shanghai are Taikoo, Jardine Matheson, Nisshin, China Merchants, Sanbei, and Ningshao. Taikoo Company has ten Yangtze River ships, such as the Huangpu, Wuchang, Wenzhou, Wusong, Wuxue, Wuhu, Changsha, Poyang, Datong, and Anqing, which run 26 to 27 flights per month. Jardine Matheson has eight ships, such as the Gonghe, Dehe, Jihe, Pinghe, Lianhe, and Xianghe, which run 20 to 21 flights per month. China Merchants has ships such as the Jiang'an, Jiangshun, Jiangxin, Jianghua, Jiangyu, Jiangtian, Jiangjing, Jiangda, and Jianguo, and the number of flights per month is the same as Taikoo and others. Sanbei has eight ships, such as the Xinningxing, Dean, Qingbo, Songbo, and Fengpu. Ningshao has two ships, the Ningshao and Ningjing. After the January 28th Incident, the Nisshin Company reduced four ships, such as the Xiangyang, Nanyang, Luoyang, and Fengyang. Therefore, the six companies operating Shanghai-Hankou flights have a total of more than 40 ships.

Lack of Both Imports and Exports

The lack of imports and exports on the Yangtze River recently is unprecedented. After the floods occurred, the various Yangtze River customer gangs suspended or stopped loading goods in order to prevent floods, resulting in a daily reduction in freight in this street. It all depends on the transit of goods from other ports, but there is also a shortage of goods coming from the Yangtze River. Recently, the Wuhu Zhenchang and other rapeseed companies packed 600,000 bags to Shanghai, which were purchased by eight oil factories in Shanghai. Because the various ships competed too fiercely for loading, the freight rates dropped sharply. Even if the price was fixed and a 5.95% commission was given, it was fortunate to be able to transport some of the goods. There are no other large quantities of goods to transport.

Decided to Suspend Scheduled Ships

The fundamental solution discussed by the six companies is to reduce the number of ships by all six companies. There is no other way. As a result, it was agreed that Taikoo Company would suspend three ships, Jardine Matheson would also suspend three ships, the China Merchants Bureau would suspend three ships, the Jiangtian, Jiangyu, and Jiangda, Ningshao would suspend the Ningjing, and Sanbei Company would also suspend one ship. Because the Nisshin Company had already reduced four Yangtze River ships after the January 28th Incident, it was not necessary to discuss it for the time being. The suspension of the other shipping companies will be implemented from July 1st.

Increase in Empty Ships Moored in the Huangpu River

Because of poor business, the upstream ships of the various Yangtze River companies that are moored in Shanghai number seven or eight. In addition, the upper and lower Yangtze River ships of the Nisshin Company that are moored in the Huangpu River and have not been sailing originally numbered 15. Except for the Daheng and Dafu, which were sold to Japan, there are still 13 ships. Now, with the addition of the reduced flights from the various companies, the number of ships moored empty on the Yangtze River will increase to more than 30.

British Pilot Hutton Will Come to Shanghai Soon

British pilot Hutton and his party of five recently came to China from the United Kingdom for a tour. They first went to Guangzhou and will come to Shanghai soon. The Guangdong Provincial Government has transferred the matter to the Shanghai Municipal Government, requesting that they be taken care of when Hutton and others arrive in Shanghai.

Shanghai-Ningbo-Suzhou Tobacco and Wine Industries Jointly Oppose the New Tax Regulations

Returning Representatives Petitioned the Tax Administration and Tax Bureau Again

Telegraphing the Ministries to Stop County Police from Assisting in Harassment

Notifying Local Industries to Refuse to Pay and Persist to the End

Shaoxing Wine Industry Association Convened an Emergency Meeting Yesterday

The Shanghai-Ningbo-Suzhou Tobacco and Wine Industries Joint Association, because the Tax Administration abolished the public sale and collection of taxes, formulated new quota regulations, which are scheduled to be implemented on July 1. The association, etc., believes that the new regulations are harsh and troublesome, and the penalties are severe. After implementation, it will have a significant impact on the commercial transportation of the two industries. Therefore, the Standing Committee of the two industries specially held a temporary emergency meeting the other day. Considering that the date of implementation of the new regulations is very urgent, and the handling procedures are urgent, it was decided to continue to send the six representatives who went to Beijing to petition to the Tax Administration and the Tax Bureau to personally state the harsh facts and request that the new regulations be abolished. They also telegraphed the Central Party Department, the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, appealing for an order to the municipal and county governments of Shanghai, Ningbo, and Suzhou to stop the Public Security Bureau from assisting in tax collection, so as to avoid conflict. The following is a record of the telegrams from various parties:

Telegramming Various Agencies

To the Central Party Department, the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing: The association, etc., previously stated that the Tax Administration illegally formulated regulations on local tobacco and wine taxes, which were harsh and troublesome, and the fines were heavy, which would wipe out commercial transportation and were inhumane. The association, etc., telegraphed on the relevant day and sent representatives Cao Gexian, Jin Xuejie, Yu Xunlu, Huang Yuming, Dai Zhuo, and Huang Wenqing to Beijing to petition. The ministries and courts received them, and the representatives stated the harsh facts of the new system. They were honored to be adopted and promised to amend them. A special article was also submitted requesting abolition. Unexpectedly, a day later, news came that was unexpected. It was reported that the Ministry of Finance ordered the seven provinces of Su, Zhejiang, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, and Fujian to start the stamp tax on tobacco and alcohol and the quota tax on local wine on July 1 this year. We are shocked. It has been found that the Tax Administration illegally formulated new tax regulations, which have been listed and presented according to law. The association, etc., publicly appointed representatives to go to Beijing to petition on behalf of all tobacco and wine merchants in Huining and Suzhou. The reason is that the new system of the bureau is illegal, the procedures are harsh, and the penalties are severe, and it cannot be absolutely recognized. If it is forcibly implemented, it will inevitably lead to incidents. Who will follow? Who will bear the blame? The association, etc., is harming the commercial transportation of the tobacco and wine industries in Huning and Suzhou. We hereby telegraphically state that we respectfully request your review and quickly order the bureau to abolish the new system, so as to avoid unfortunate incidents. We will be very grateful, and we hope to receive a telegram in reply to comfort us. Zhang Dalian, the chairman of the United Association of Tobacco and Wine Industries in Huining and Suzhou, Standing Committee members Jin Yunjie, Dai Zhuan, Jin Jiayue, and Chen Weiwen, Chen Liangyu, the chairman of the United Association of Tobacco and Wine Industries in Huining and Suzhou, and Standing Committee members Yu Xunlu, Zhang Suhou, Cao Gexian, and Shen Weiting, bow, Yan Yin.

Submitting Documents to the Tax Administration

The six representatives petitioned, and the document submitted to the Tax Administration stated: "For the sake of urgently requesting the abolition of the local tobacco and wine tax regulations, and the exemption of local tobacco and wine taxes to help merchants in difficulty and avoid disputes. It has been found that domestic tobacco and wine have been taxed through public sales for more than ten years, and merchants have not been inconvenienced. Recently, it was heard that your office plans to abolish public sales and formulate regulations on the special tax on the local tobacco industry and the quota tax on local wine, which are scheduled to be implemented on July 1. The association, etc., believes that the matter is related to the burden of the two industries and endangers the livelihood, and appointed Cao Gexian, Jin Wenjie, Yu Xunlu, Huang Yuming, Dai Zhuan, and Huang Wenqing as representatives of all the industries in Shanghai, Ningbo, and Suzhou to go to Beijing to petition the Central Party Department, the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance to clarify the harshness of the new tax and request the suspension of its implementation, and to submit it to the Ministry of Finance for review. The representatives returned to Shanghai to report that they met Secretary Chen of the Legislative Yuan, Counselor Chen of the Executive Yuan, and Secretary-General Yang of the Ministry of Finance. The representatives detailed the new system, which was harsh and the fines were severe. Once implemented, not only would the burden increase suddenly, but even the slightest carelessness would lead to legal problems. It can be seen that the local tobacco and local wine would be wiped out, which is equivalent to promoting foreign goods and destroying domestic products. At a time when the rural economy is bankrupt, rescuing is feared to be too late, so how can we bear to harass it again? We request that you quickly order the abolition of the new system to help merchants in difficulty. Responsible personnel from the upper-level agencies replied that the case was handled by the Tax Administration, so they should explain it in detail to the office to determine the course of action, so the representatives returned to Shanghai to report to the superiors for review and handling. It has been found that the association, etc., publicly appointed representatives to go to Beijing to petition on behalf of all tobacco and wine merchants in Shanghai, Ningbo, and Suzhou. The reason is that the new system of local tobacco and wine taxes proposed by your office is harsh, and the penalties are severe, and it cannot be absolutely recognized. If it is forcibly implemented, then all tobacco and wine merchants in Shanghai, Ningbo, and Suzhou still have hearts and blood, and they will naturally refuse to pay and persist to the end. Any sacrifice will be made at all costs. It will inevitably lead to incidents. Who will take the lead? Who will bear the blame? The association, etc., is preventing disasters before they happen and stopping harm before it comes, so we have to run around and shout out. According to the previous report, in addition to ordering the representatives to visit and state the case, we should present the document to respectfully request your Excellency to grant us an audience, adopt our humble opinions, and admire your Excellency's impartiality and integrity. We will definitely resolutely abolish the aforementioned new system to help merchants in difficulty and avoid disputes. The time is pressing, and we cannot choose our words carefully. We are very anxious to wait for orders." We respectfully present this to Xie, the director of the Tax Administration of the Ministry of Finance, and the content of the presentation to the director of the Jiangsu Stamp Tobacco and Wine Tax Bureau is the same, which is omitted here.

Letter to Fellow Professionals in Various Counties

Regarding the matter of Directly Addressing: Our association and others have investigated that the Tax Bureau has abolished the old regulations and established new ones, scheduled to take effect on July 1st. This matter concerns the burden on both industries and endangers livelihoods. We dispatched Cao Gexian and five others as representatives to petition in Beijing, and also submitted requests to higher-level agencies to abolish the new system. Now, according to the report from the representatives who returned to Shanghai, they met with Secretary Chen of the Legislative Yuan, Counselor Chen of the Executive Yuan, and Secretary-General Yang of the Ministry of Finance, detailing the onerous and troublesome nature of the new system. The responsible personnel of the higher-level agencies replied that the case was mainly handled by the Tax Bureau and that the issue should be explained in detail to the bureau to determine the course of action. The representatives returned and went to the Tax Bureau and the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau to petition. Although they did not get a satisfactory result, the responsible personnel of the bureau verbally agreed to discuss and amend the regulations. However, the date of implementation is approaching, and we fear that the tax collection sub-bureaus in various counties will cater to the authorities and enforce the regulations. If this occurs, the tobacco and alcohol merchants of Shanghai, Ningbo, and Suzhou will undoubtedly refuse to pay and persevere to the end, regardless of any sacrifice. We are issuing this order to prevent disasters before they happen and to stop harm before it arrives. In addition to submitting reports to the Shanghai and Ningbo Municipal Governments and the Jiangsu Provincial Government, we are also sending letters to various county governments, instructing the Public Security Bureaus, district offices, and others to temporarily suspend assistance to avoid disputes. Furthermore, we are sending this special letter to you, hoping that your association will investigate and, before the Legislative Yuan, Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance issue a clear resolution on this case, if any tax authorities harass and disturb the merchants, first report to the nearest chamber of commerce for assistance. At the same time, send a telegram to our association to strive for a justified resolution and alleviate the pain. Attached is a letter to the county government, which your association should designate a representative to deliver in person for negotiation. Respectfully, to the Tobacco and Alcohol Industry Association of a certain county. Attached: one official letter.

Submission to Provincial and Municipal Governments

Submission regarding the unauthorized formulation of local tobacco and alcohol tax regulations by the Tax Bureau, scheduled for implementation, fearing coercive actions and inciting incidents, requesting the authorities to order the Public Security Bureau and district offices to temporarily suspend assistance, to alleviate merchants' difficulties and avoid disputes. We, the association, previously heard that the Ministry of Finance's Tax Bureau is changing regulations regarding the tobacco and alcohol tax rates for the 22nd year, revoking the public sales system, and revising the special tax on local tobacco leaves and the fixed tax on local alcohol. The articles are onerous and the fines are severe. Once implemented, it will not only increase the burden sharply, but also lead to legal troubles with the slightest carelessness. The local tobacco and alcohol will soon be wiped out, which will encourage foreign goods and destroy domestic products. At a time when the rural economy is bankrupt, even rescue efforts are not enough; how can we bear further harassment? Our association and others have resolved in a general meeting to appoint six representatives to go to Beijing and petition the Central Party Headquarters, the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance to abolish the bureau's unauthorized new system. According to the report from the representatives who returned to Shanghai, they have obtained the permission of the higher-level agencies, and the bureau's newly established regulations will be submitted to the Yuan and Ministry, which have the power to review and revise them for correction. Therefore, the representatives returned to Shanghai to report for examination and handling. According to the investigation, the bureau's new system is cumbersome and punitive, and we absolutely cannot accept it. If it is forcibly implemented, the tobacco and alcohol merchants in Shanghai, Ningbo, and Suzhou will undoubtedly refuse to pay and persevere to the end, regardless of any sacrifice. We are afraid that the bureau will act arbitrarily and order the Public Security Bureau and its district offices to send police to intimidate us, which will inevitably incite incidents. Whose fault will it be? To prevent disasters before they happen and to stop harm before it arrives, in addition to submitting reports to the Shanghai and Ningbo Municipal Governments and sending letters to various county governments, we specially submit this document requesting your authority to examine and approve, and promptly order the Public Security Bureau to notify its district offices that before the Legislative Yuan, Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance issue a clear resolution on this case, if the Tax Bureau and the Tobacco and Alcohol Tax Bureau request police assistance, they should temporarily suspend it to alleviate merchants' difficulties and avoid disputes. We also request instructions to follow, as it is for the public good. Also, the letters to various county governments have the same content and are omitted here.

Shaoxing Wine Industry Conference

The Shaoxing Wine Industry Association convened its 26th emergency executive committee meeting yesterday afternoon. Ding Jinsheng chaired the meeting, and all executive committee members performed the rituals as usual. Proposals: (1) Regarding the Tax Bureau's change of the public sales system to a fixed tax on local alcohol, the newly established tax regulations will be implemented on July 1st. It was argued that the regulations are onerous and the tax is increased several times, which is unbearable for merchants. Moreover, due to the impact of the war, there has been no recovery. The bureau's sudden implementation of detailed regulations will destroy the livelihood of our industry. All executive committee members unanimously resolved to send a telegram to the Ministry of Finance, the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, and Chairman Chiang in the capital, requesting a postponement of the harsh taxation to alleviate merchants' difficulties. In addition to submitting requests to the ministry and Yuan, they also prepared documents to submit to the Tax Bureau, the Municipal Government, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce. As a public association, we should fulfill our duties and strive for justice, and never protect the authorities. The meeting adjourned after the discussion. The telegram to the Executive Yuan stated: "To the Executive Yuan: Recently, we heard that the Tax Bureau has completely abolished the liquor public sales system implemented in the seven provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Hubei, Henan, and other provinces over the years, and promulgated 40 new articles of the local alcohol fixed tax regulations and the local alcohol fixed tax rate table, which will be implemented on July 1st of this year. We found that the articles of the regulations are cumbersome and do not conform to commercial practices. The tax rate table imposes excessive taxes, which is difficult for the people to bear. Once implemented, domestic products will inevitably be gradually destroyed, and imported wines will be sold smoothly, which will endanger the people's livelihood and social stability. We request that your President promptly stop this and temporarily postpone the implementation. We urgently pray. The Shanghai Shaoxing Wine Industry Association."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Resolves to Sanction Stores That Do Not Join the Association

Please Order a Trial Chapter

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously submitted a report to the Social Affairs Bureau, stating: "The purpose of organizing a trade association is to organize the public and coordinate business operations. However, there is no clear provision in the law. Although trade associations have been established, countless cunning people believe that joining the association requires obeying uniform prices, which loses the freedom of will, and they are reluctant to move forward. Moreover, they widely publicize this, causing those who have joined the association to be forced to withdraw, which makes it impossible for the association to exert its functions and implement its purpose. Moreover, there are no sanctions in the law for those who withdraw from the association, fail to pay membership fees, or do not join the association. If this continues, it will make it impossible for those who have not organized to organize, and those who have organized will collapse. The proposed measures are as follows: (1) Order all trades to join the association; (2) Request the Legislative Yuan to add a provision in the Trade Association Law that requires joining a trade association; (3) Request the Legislative Yuan to transfer to the law enforcement agencies to order businesses that do not join the association to suspend business. Representatives of the copper-iron machinery industry, the Chinese and foreign grocery industry, the shoe-leather nail-last industry, and the cosmetics industry also made similar proposals to the meeting. The key to the difficulty of this matter lies in the fact that it must be in accordance with legal principles and have a compulsory effect. The compulsory measures proposed by the association, etc., have been forwarded to your bureau and have been recorded. However, there are relevant legal issues involved. The association has attached its opinions and stated that the first item of the measures proposed by the laundry industry association has already been included in Article 7 of the amended Trade Association Law, and the second level seems to be hindered by many laws and regulations. The association also found that among the various industries, only the rice shop industry has mostly joined the association, because the Public Works Department's donation license is transferred by the association on behalf of the association. Merchants seek this convenience and gather unexpectedly. If we can imitate its method, and designate the association to handle all special events related to the government, then the effect of Dong Quan is better than oppression. If your bureau can formulate a special chapter for trial within the scope of its authority, it will be more convenient. After being submitted to the general meeting for a vote, it was resolved to continue the previous case and submit a strong request to your bureau for examination and processing. It is for the public good. Respectfully submitted to the Shanghai Social Affairs Bureau."

Han Shengxiang, a 15-year-old female worker from Shaoxing at No. 175 Meiya Second Silk Weaving Factory on Jiaotong Road, Zhabei, was sent to Baolong Hospital on Baike Road for treatment at 1:00 AM on the 29th by her companions Wang Hefen, Qiu Guifen, Xue Meihua, and Qiu Genfen. Zhu Xingen Released from Abduction

Two Kidnappers Arrested

On the evening of the third day of the ninth lunar month of the previous year, Zhu Shuzhi's 14-year-old eldest son Zhu Xingen and 13-year-old second son Zhu Liangen were kidnapped by more than ten kidnappers from the Lijiashuyuan Township in Pudong. A huge ransom was demanded for their release. On April 13th of this year, after several contacts with the kidnappers, the victim offered 2,500 yuan and only redeemed his youngest son Liangen. Xingen was still hidden in the kidnappers' den, and a huge ransom was demanded. No agreement has been reached so far. Jin Jiulin, an inspector of the special agency of the French Concession Police, learned that the kidnappers were hiding in Room 36 of the Hongxiang Hotel on Avenue Edward VII in the Public Concession. At noon yesterday, they opened Room 42 of the Siming Hotel on Xizilaihuo Street in the French Concession to negotiate the ransom. Inspector Jin immediately led detectives Zhang Ziying, Zhou Yaoting, Zhou Bingcheng, Bao Tan Qin Youyu, Cai Jinzhang, Ma Yizhi, and others in disguise to the scene. First, they arrested Yang Linsheng (42 years old) from Pudong, a kidnapper, in front of No. 616 Xizang Road. Then, they arrested Yang Hanchu (23 years old) from Pudong in the Hongxiang Hotel. They intercepted the hostage Zhu Xingen at the intersection of Nanjing Road and Guangxi Road and took them back to the police station. First, the hostage was handed over to the victim, and Yang and others were detained for interrogation.

Continued Hearing of the Case of Actor Zhao Ruquan Accused of Embezzling Huge Sums

Actor Zhao Ruquan is a shareholder and cashier of the Sanxing Stage. Recently, Zhou Bingchen, a shareholder and former manager of the stage, discovered that Zhao had embezzled a huge sum of money. He collected evidence and hired lawyers Chen Tingrui, Yuan Yang'an, and Du Jimei to report to the police station, ordering detective Chen Yonggui to arrest Zhao and file a public lawsuit. The First Special District Court has conducted several trials, and the details have been recorded in previous reports. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Feng Shide continued the trial in the Criminal Court No. 1. The lawyer of the police station, Ru Bao Yi, stated that since the accountant Zhao Zuwei reviewed the accounts and reported to the court, the defendant requested permission for his accountant, Jiang Wanping, to re-examine them. With the court's permission, Jiang's report has now been submitted to the court. If it has been submitted, please issue a copy for review. Judge Feng then issued Jiang's report and questioned Zhao Ruquan. According to Zhao's accountant's report, the Sanxing Stage should have more than 60,000 yuan in cash, but the passbooks of the Siming Bank are over-deducted. In total, the amount is only 40,000 yuan, which is less than 20,000 yuan. Where did it come from? Zhao replied, "All the money I received has been presented to the court. The rest of the money is in the outside account room and has nothing to do with me." He was also asked that the income of the Sanxing Stage has been huge in recent years. If it is all deposited in the bank, the interest alone must be considerable. However, the interest in the folding you presented to the court is extremely levied, so whether the income is deposited in the bank. Reply, "I am extremely busy, so sometimes the money I receive cannot be immediately handed over to the bank. I will hand it over a few days later. Sometimes, because I need to use the money, I will not hand it over to the bank." At this time, the accountant Jiang stood up and gave a detailed report on the review of the accounts, which lasted a long time. After the report was completed, the court asked Zhao's accountant what opinions he had on Jiang Wanping's report. Zhao's accountant replied that Jiang's report had just been received and could not be read in detail, so he could not comment for the time being and would submit a written report to the court tomorrow. Judge Feng then questioned Zhao Ruquan, saying that according to what you said, the money on the deposit book is still more than 3,000 yuan short of the cash that should be deposited. Where is this money now? Zhao replied, "It is all in the iron cabinet of the Sanxing Stage." The lawyer Jiang Yiping immediately stood up and said that this money has now been brought. Then, he presented the money and said that Zhao Ruquan is so stupid that it is ridiculous. He keeps the money he receives separate and does not combine it. It can be seen that he has no bad intentions. He also presented an account book, saying that this account book is for the collection and payment of money between the outside account room and Zhao Ruquan, and this book is very helpful to the defendant. The lawyer of the police station, Ru Bao Yi, immediately stood up and said that the account book presented by the defendant today was not mentioned before, and it was not presented until today, which is too late. As for the silver dollars presented in the case, it is said that they are still sealed and taken out of the iron cabinet. Since no one has seen the money before and it is hidden in the iron cabinet, what style is it? How can you know that it is still sealed and not taken out temporarily? Only God knows this. Judge Feng then questioned Zhao and others point by point in the accounts until dusk, and then ordered the hearing to be rescheduled.

Execution of the Three Kidnappers in the Sun Yangru Case

The Three Criminals Appeared Composed

Showing No Signs of Fear

The kidnappers, Shandong natives Yang Baofu, 37 years old, Tang Jinsheng, 47 years old, and Wang Yaohua, 37 years old, were involved in a case where they conspired with accomplices on December 14th of last year, around 4 PM, to kidnap Sun Yangru, a comprador from Anhui working for the Fufeng Flour Company at 25 Renji Road, near the Xiejiao Road on Tongfu Road. They hid him in a den on Fuxu Road (Avenue Foch) near Laoer Road (Route Tenant de la Tour) and demanded a large ransom. After the case occurred, they were apprehended by Chief Detective Ling Liankui, Detective Liu Shaokui, and Detective Zhou Honglin of the Chinese Detective Division of the General Inspectorate, along with Yang Baofu and others. The hostage was rescued, and they were handed over to the First Special District Court. After repeated investigations and trials, they were sentenced to death. The judgment was submitted to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval, and the order for execution was issued. Yesterday morning, the execution was carried out. The police escorted Yang and the others to the Third Criminal Court of the Special Court, where Judge Yang Shanzeng presided. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the police, presented the case details, along with the confession and judgment documents. The court ordered the three criminals to be brought forward. The criminals appeared calm and composed, showing no signs of fear. Judge Shen announced, "You have been convicted of kidnapping and sentenced to death. Today is the day of execution. Do you have any final words or matters to communicate to your families?" Yang Baofu stated that he had seen his wife and two sisters at the courthouse entrance and requested to speak with them. The court declared, "You must state your intentions directly." Yang said, "After my death, I ask my wife to come and collect my body for cremation, and I request that a letter be sent to my sister Chen Genqing at 55 Hanzhong Lane, Hanzhong Road, Zhabei, to teach my nephew to be law-abiding in his business and not associate with bad friends, so that he may have someone to rely on in the future." Tang and Wang stated that they had no final words or family matters to communicate. Judge Shen then ordered the Chinese and foreign detectives to take the three criminals down, put them in a car, and transport them along with the case files and photos to the execution ground in front of the Second Prison in Caohejing. Prosecutor Cao, commissioned by the local court, arrived at the scene and ordered the bailiffs to bring forward Yang and the other two criminals, verify their identities, restrain them according to the law, and carry out the execution by firing squad.

Wang Yansong's Letter to Mayor Wu

Ban Nude Body Movement

= The Nation is in Difficulty; Urge Calm and Hard Work

Do not Open the Door to Licentiousness and Extravagance =

Wang Yansong, Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce and General Manager of the Silk Industry Bank, stated that it had been reported that a nude body movement in Hong Kong was planning to come to Shanghai, which would have a profound and detrimental impact on public morals. Yesterday, he sent a letter to the Mayor, requesting a ban. He also sent letters to various organizations, urging a unified stance. The original letter stated: "Mayor, I am writing to you after reading yesterday's news about the rumored arrival of a nude body movement from Hong Kong. I have read reports stating that this movement originated after the European War, advocated by a group of people with the intention of braving frost and dew to strengthen their bodies. However, according to national laws and regulations, any person who appears naked in streets or public gatherings is considered to be in violation of police regulations. This personal, curious behavior is not allowed by national laws and regulations. Moreover, there are many proper ways to exercise. Shanghai is one of the most important cities in the country and also a den of vice. Indulgence and absurdity are rampant. Those with weak wills are easily attracted to novelty and blindly follow. Furthermore, hearing that the proponents of this movement are foreigners, they will want to imitate and falsely claim it as civilization. If this is the case, humanity will regress to ancient times, and the corruption of morals will be led by this movement. In the past, film showings that appealed to sensuality were criticized and banned. How would this nude body movement compare to films that appeal to sensuality? It is self-evident. The nation is in difficulty; we should guide the people towards calmness and hard work, not open the door to licentiousness and extravagance. These foreigners are trying to organize a branch in Shanghai, perhaps exploiting our weaknesses and viewing it as a commercial venture. The way to govern a country is to balance flexibility and rigidity according to the times. In the past, Ms. Sanger's advocacy of birth control was met with criticism in Japan because it was incompatible with their national conditions. Therefore, no matter how foreigners promote this movement, it is not suitable for our country today, especially not in a city known as a den of vice. I hereby respectfully submit this letter, requesting that you investigate and prohibit it. At the same time, I am writing to the concession authorities, requesting them to take similar action. This would truly be a public service."

Display Arrangement

We plan to ask domestic and foreign goods factories to donate gifts to be distributed to the guests as a form of advertising and remembrance. We admire your esteemed factory for its excellent products and widespread reputation. We are sending a representative to respectfully request your generous donation of gifts to attract interest."

Reply from He and Cai

(1) He Bingxian, Director of the International Trade Bureau, replied to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, stating: "I am writing in response to your esteemed letter. I have received your kind invitation to serve as a member of the China National Silk Exhibition Committee. I am grateful and honored. I will do my best to fulfill this role." (2) Cai Wuji, Director of the Commodity Inspection Bureau, replied: "I have received your esteemed letter inviting me to serve as a member of the China National Silk Exhibition Committee. I am aware of my limited abilities and am hesitant to accept. However, as it concerns the promotion of domestic silk, I will strive to follow your instructions. I am writing this letter to inform you and hope you will take note."

Huaxin Participates

The Huaxin Printing and Dyeing Company has produced excellent and innovative products that are very fashionable. The factory is enthusiastically preparing to participate in the exhibition and has prepared dozens of the latest products to display at the venue.

Wang Yansong Convenes

Meeting of Representatives of Merchants in the National Goods Market

Mr. Wang Yansong, Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, Director of the Commodity Display Center, and General Manager of the Shanghai Silk Bank, convened a meeting of representatives of merchants in the National Goods Market at the dining area of the market at 12 noon on the 24th. More than 40 representatives attended. Mr. Wang delivered a speech, stating, "Since I took office as Director of the Commodity Display Center, it has been almost a year. Due to my heavy workload, I have had little contact with the representatives, and I have not made any achievements within the organization. I am deeply ashamed. I believe that in recent years, the domestic silk industry has been affected by the dumping policies of foreign goods, leading to a decline in business, making it difficult for factories to survive, and increasing the number of unemployed workers. The social situation is becoming increasingly unstable. If we do not seek a solution, the harm will be unimaginable. Therefore, I convened a joint meeting of the Executive Committee and Supervisory Committee of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce on February 24th to discuss the issue. It was decided that the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce National Goods Market, the Shanghai Silk Industry Association, the Shanghai Electric Wire Factory Association, and the Shanghai Silk Bank would jointly organize the China National Silk Exhibition and use the third floor of the Commodity Display Center as the exhibition venue. The opening is scheduled for July 9th. At that time, there will be a dazzling array of brocades and silks gathered in one room for public viewing, demonstrating the promotion of national goods. This exhibition bears the responsibility of revitalizing the national silk industry. If it is not handled properly, promoted effectively, and carried out proactively, it will be difficult to ensure that the national silk industry will be revived after the exhibition. If other industries are organized separately, it will not be difficult for our national goods to develop from this point. Furthermore, at the opening of this exhibition, I hope that the representatives will select more high-quality national goods and sell them at low prices to support the promotion of national goods." The representatives then delivered speeches in succession. Finally, the report on the conclusion of the issuance of profit coupons in the market was made. The meeting adjourned at around 4 PM.

Wang Bamei, Female Bandit under Tai Bao Ashu, Apprehended

= Wang Transported Guns and Ammunition for Yu Weitang's Robbery of a Ship

Her Husband, Shi Dianyuan, Is Still at Large and Has Not Been Arrested =

| Yesterday, the Case Was Transferred to the Water Police |

Tai Bao Ashu, the bandit leader of Taihu Lake, had a large number of followers who formed gangs and disturbed travelers, robbed passing ships, kidnapped people for ransom, committed arson, and did everything evil. The authorities dispatched troops to suppress them repeatedly, but they could not be completely eliminated. It was not until the previous year that the Water Police successively arrested Tai Bao Ashu and other important members of his gang and sentenced them to death. During the interrogation, Gao Guiyou, Cai Axiao, Wu Yaogen, and others confessed that their accomplices, Shi Dianyuan and his mistress Wang Bamei, were also important members of the gang. They confessed that Wang Bamei had transported four rifles during the robbery of a ship in Yu Weitang. However, Shi and the others fled to other cities after the case occurred, and their whereabouts were uncertain, so they remained at large and could not be arrested. Recently, Luo Daokun, the captain of the Third Team of the First District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police, discovered that Shi and his wife were hiding at 1605, Lane 3, Fude Fang, Hed Road, in the Public Concession. Therefore, on the afternoon of the previous day, they notified the Jing'an Temple Police Station and secretly went with Chinese and foreign detectives to arrest them. However, Shi Dianyuan fled, and only his mistress Wang Bamei, also known as Zhang Wushi, was arrested. A colored photograph of the woman was also seized, which was the same as the photograph seized from Tai Bao Ashu's bandit ship in Jiaxing. She was taken to the police station and transferred to the women's prison. Yesterday morning, she was escorted to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. First, a Chinese detective described the circumstances of the arrest, and then Captain Luo Daokun submitted an official document stating that the real name of the defendant was Wang Bamei, the mistress of Shi Dianyuan, and a member of Tai Bao Ashu's gang. She had committed serious crimes in the past, as confessed by Cai Axiao and others. The confessions of Cai and others, along with the seized photographs, were submitted to the court, requesting permission to transfer her for interrogation. Zhang Wushi claimed that she lived in her hometown of Pinghu and had an elderly mother and a six-year-old child at home. Her husband, Zhang Jinsheng, died of illness on November 4th of last year. After her husband's death, she took her young child and came to Shanghai by boat. Because she had no way to make a living, she worked as a female tailor. She first lived in Rongji Lane, Weihaiwei Road, and moved to Fude Fang, Hed Road, in April, renting the front building for nine yuan a month. There were no men, only her mother and son living together. She did not know Shi Dianyuan and the others. The seized photographs were taken in March at a photo studio in Ba Xian Qiao and hung on the wall. The detectives took them away yesterday. She was a woman from the countryside, how could she be involved with bandits and transport guns? She asked for a fair judgment. Captain Luo stated that only one colored photograph was found during the arrest and that her clothes rack was full of men's clothes, apparently belonging to Shi. Lawyer Li Zhishan stated that the statements made by the defendant Zhang Wushi today were unreliable. Furthermore, the Provincial Public Security Team had already submitted photographs and confessions from accomplices, so there was sufficient evidence. The police did not object to the transfer. Judge Wu Tingqi approved the transfer of Zhang Wushi, also known as Wang Bamei, to Captain Luo Daokun of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police for interrogation.

Reuters Messenger Attacked by Enemy

Jiang Shounan, a 20-year-old messenger for Reuters from Changshu, was attacked at the intersection of Edward Road and Sichuan Road at around 0:30 AM this morning. He was ordered to deliver a telegram to a lane on the Rue Ratard in the French Concession. However, it was midnight, and the area was desolate and dark. Suddenly, his enemy attacked him from the dark with an axe, striking his neck. The wound was about half an inch deep, and he bled profusely. The assailant took the opportunity to flee. After being injured, Jiang hired a car to return to the office, where his colleagues accompanied him to Renji Hospital for treatment. According to Jiang, the assailant was named Wu Gengsheng, who had previously been a messenger at the same office. Wu was dismissed for attempting to steal a bicycle and sell it for personal use, which was reported by Jiang Shounan. This attack was motivated by revenge.

Wang Shuangxi, Troubled by Finances, Commits Suicide

Wang Shuangxi, a farmer in his late thirties from Changshu, came to Shanghai alone on the 26th and stayed at Room 99 on the upper floor of the Dongnan Hotel in Taiyuan Fang, French Concession. He had a history of opium addiction and had quit once. After arriving in Shanghai, he felt unwell and went out to smoke opium for several days, adding to his expenses. On the afternoon of the previous day, at around 3:30 PM, he felt financially strapped and desperate, so he secretly ingested a large amount of raw opium and committed suicide. He was discovered and sent to Renji Hospital by streetcar, but he died at 3:45 AM the next morning. The hospital reported the death to the Greater Cuckoo Clock Police Station, and detective Wang Licheng was dispatched to the scene. The body was transported to Tongren Fuyuan Hall and will be examined by the court this morning.

Coal and Stone Barge Industry Association Holds Joint Meeting of Executive and Supervisory Committees

Zhu Tongfu and Five Others Elected as Standing Committee Members

The Coal and Stone Barge Industry Association of this city convened its first joint meeting of the Second Executive and Supervisory Committees at 3 PM yesterday. Fourteen executive committee members and two supervisory committee members attended. Hu Xiangbao was elected as temporary chairman. The meeting first discussed ways to regulate freight rates to maintain business. Finally, five standing committee members were elected: Zhu Tongfu, Yuan Genquan, Hu Xiangbao, Yu Qingyun, and Zhang Caixing. Zhu Tongfu was elected as chairman of the committee. The meeting adjourned at around 5 PM.

British Man, Mr. Creighton's Body Found in Huangpu River

Around noon the other day, two Chinese police officers from the Water Patrol Team recovered a floating body from the Huangpu River, about 150 yards east of Peng Road, upstream from the China Merchants Bureau Pier. The body was identified as that of a Westerner. A search of his pockets revealed no papers, only a few coins and a pair of glasses. However, the cuffs of his shirt had the English name "Creighton." His clothes were neat, and there were no signs of injury. It was later confirmed that the body was that of Mr. Creighton, a long-time member of the Race Club, who was 62 years old. In recent years, he had been a member of the Municipal Council. About a week ago, he was staying with his family on the third floor of the apartment building at 753 Yu Yuan Road. On the evening of the 1st of this week, he was seen at the Race Club around 8 PM. After that, he disappeared. Based on the condition of his remains, he had been in the water for several days. Yesterday, the coroner examined the body at the Public Morgue. After Mr. Wilkinson confirmed that it was the body of Mr. Creighton, the inquest was adjourned to July 7th.

Lost Girl on Zixia Road

Yesterday, police officer Liu Jinli of the First Precinct, Third Station of the Municipal Public Security Bureau found a lost girl on Zixia Road outside the Datongmen Gate. The girl was about 4 or 5 years old and spoke with a Ningbo accent. She was wearing a plaid short shirt and striped pants, barefoot, and wearing patterned cloth shoes. She was taken back to the station, but she refused to speak, so her name and address could not be determined. Instructions were given to wait for her family to come and claim her.

Bank of China Inspection Report

Sixty-Fourth Time

The Sixty-Fourth Inspection Report of the Shanghai Bank of China Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee states: "The members of this committee, along with the commissioned accountants, inspected the issuance and exchange reserve vault of the Shanghai Bank of China Main Branch, according to the rules of this committee, on June 25th, 1933. The Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance also joined the inspection. The results of the inspection are as follows: Total amount of exchange coupons issued: 10,473,7183 yuan. This includes: Amount issued by the Main Branch: 63,724,551 yuan. Amount used by affiliated branches: 1,820,0808 yuan. Amount used by various banks and firms: 22,811,124 yuan. Except for the amount used by various banks and firms, which will be inspected separately according to the original method, the inspection of the amount used by the Main Branch and affiliated branches is as follows: Amount issued by the Main Branch and used by affiliated branches: 81,925,359 yuan. Amount of exchange coupon reserves for the Main Branch and affiliated branches: 81,925,359 yuan. This includes: Cash reserves: 54,480,685.33 yuan. Guarantee reserves: 27,444,673.67 yuan. The cash reserves account for 60% of the total, and the guarantee reserves account for 40% of the total. Both items were inspected and found to be accurate. In accordance with Article 5 of the rules, this report is hereby formally submitted. June 25th, 1933. Xu Kan, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance; Wang Yansong, Pei Yunqing, Representatives of the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce; Tang Shoumin, Ye Fuxiao, Representatives of the Shanghai Banking Association; Li Jisheng, Chuan Songnian, Representatives of the Shanghai Money Trade Association; Li Fusun, Wang Bingcheng, Representatives of the Coupon-Issuing Banks and Firms; Xu Ji, Ye Zhuotang, Zhou Zongliang, Li Zhilian, Representatives of the Supervisors of the Bank of China; Accountant Wang Zikang."

Calligraphy and Painting News

Mr. Chang Zhuozhi of Sichuan is skilled in calligraphy and painting. He has come to Shanghai, and the number of people seeking his work is increasing daily. His painting fees are $5 per foot for hanging scrolls, $6 per foot for large central paintings, $4 per foot for screen panels, and $6 per piece for fan and album leaves. Calligraphy fees are half of that. Submissions can be sent to Yu Ji Zhan Hengshunchang, Maijiaquan, Wuma Road, Rongjili, Shanghai.

Pu Yong's calligraphy, Pu Yong, also known as Ju Ling, from Jiading, is the son of the late great calligrapher Mr. Pu Jishao. With deep family roots, he is well-versed in calligraphy. He is proficient in regular, cursive, seal, and clerical scripts, as well as inscriptions on ancient bronze vessels. His clerical script is particularly outstanding, comparable to Mei Xi's Yuan Sou, establishing a major school. Taking advantage of his spare time from teaching during the summer vacation, he is selling his calligraphy at a reasonable price. Those who admire his work should not miss this opportunity. Please inquire with major fan shops for his fee schedule.

Wen Yan Shan Guan Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition. The owner of Wen Yan Shan Guan has loved painting and calligraphy since childhood. Over the decades, he has collected over a thousand pieces of ancient and modern celebrity works, including couplets, central paintings, hanging scrolls, hand scrolls, and album leaves, all rare and exquisite items. Starting yesterday, they are being exhibited publicly on the fourth floor of the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow Association on Xizang Road, and he is willing to part with them to share with fellow enthusiasts. It is said that over a thousand people visited on the first day, and many people were eager to purchase them on the spot due to the authenticity and reasonable prices. Those with a passion for calligraphy and painting should not miss this opportunity.

Free Malaria Relief Plaster. Mr. Zhu Zilian, No. 15, Duojia Lane, Duojiali, Nanshi, is widely distributing his family's secret recipe of malaria relief plaster to patients for free. No payment is required upon request. Requests by mail with postage attached (2 cents for local, 5 cents for out-of-town) will be promptly sent. It is also available at the main entrance and side entrances of the New World. According to patients who have used it, the plaster has a miraculous effect with sure results and is especially suitable for children who dislike taking medicine.

Zhabei District Farmers' Association Establishes Free Clinic. As the hot summer arrives, it is easy to fall ill if one is not careful. Zhabei has not recovered from the ravages of war, and farmers are struggling financially. If they fall ill, they will not be able to afford medical treatment. In view of this, the Shanghai Zhabei District Farmers' Association has actively raised funds to establish a free clinic near the Gongyu Bridge on Xibaoxing Road. Since its opening, a steady stream of poor and sick people have sought treatment. However, the location of Xibaoxing Road is somewhat remote, making it difficult to reach the public. Therefore, the association has made efforts to add a clinic inside the Baoshan Hospital at the intersection of Baoshan Road and Qiujiang Road, and has hired famous doctors such as Yu Kewen and Zhou Fucang to provide free medical services. Farmers and the poor in Zhabei can enjoy free treatment if they fall ill.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather on the Shandong coast is cloudy with localized heavy fog. The wind is from the northeast. It is cloudy in this area and over the East China Sea, with heavy fog and cyclones, and there is the possibility of sudden strong gusts of wind and rain, due to the current hurricane in northern Guangzhou weakening, creating a low pressure system moving northeast or east-northeast. The middle reaches of the Yangtze River are cloudy with heavy fog and northeast winds. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the temperature in this area was a high of 80.6 and a low of 74.7. On the same day last year, the high was 82.4 and the low was 68.9.

Letter

Education News

Important News

Peking University's Lingering Issues Resolved

▲ Schools of Commerce and Law Can Still Enroll Students Next Year

▲ High School Students Transferred to Excellent Middle Schools

(Peiping, 30th) All lingering issues at Peking University have been resolved. High school students will be transferred to excellent middle schools. The schools will focus on quality after being converted into specialized schools. The schools of commerce and law can still enroll new students next year.

Ministry of Education Plans to Formulate Policies and Cultural Laws for Researching Border Regions

(Nanjing, 30th) At the request of the Ministry of Military Affairs, the Ministry of Education plans to formulate policies and cultural laws for researching border regions: (1) Compile reference books on the history, geography, politics, economics, and religion of various ethnic groups in the border regions, and compile textbooks for secondary schools to be listed as required subjects; (2) Establish specialized departments in universities across the country to study border languages, and conduct special examinations after graduation. Graduates with good results will be assigned to various border areas by the government; (3) Universities should organize border inspection teams, with travel expenses subsidized by the government; (4) The government will formulate incentive measures for all writings related to the border regions; (5) Compile textbooks in both Han-Mongolian, Han-Tibetan, and Han-Hui languages and distribute them to various border areas; (6) Order major printing houses in the country to equip themselves to print various languages. The ministry believes that items (1) and (3) fall within the scope of university education and should be handled by the schools based on their respective scientific disciplines, talents, and financial resources. On the 30th, an order was issued to all public and private universities and colleges to comply and report.

Ministry of Education Orders Bookstores to Submit Books

And Collect Local Chronicles

(Nanjing, 30th) Since the Ministry of Education previously announced regulations for submitting newly published books, only Shanghai has been urged to have bookstores submit them. Now, the ministry has ordered all provincial departments and bureaus to order bookstores to submit all books published in the past three years that have not been submitted. If they fail to submit them by the deadline, they will be handled in accordance with Article 5 of the regulations. The Ministry of Education issued a notice to all provincial departments and bureaus to collect local chronicles and send them directly to the ministry.

Ministry of Education Supervisors Complete Inspection of Education in Henan

The Ministry of Education previously sent supervisors Zhou Bangdao and Dai Xia to Henan to inspect various types of education for more than a month. Supervisor Zhou Bangdao returned to Beijing on June 29th, and Dai Xia will also return to the ministry in the near future. The inspection report must be compiled jointly by supervisors Zhou and Dai based on their respective inspection situations and will be released in a few days. It is reported that the two supervisors jointly inspected Kaifeng, Zhengzhou, Luoyang, and other places. For the separate routes, Dai inspected northern and eastern Henan, and Zhou inspected southern and western Henan, passing through approximately 20 counties. They visited many primary and secondary schools and also visited several universities. They also separately inspected educational administrative agencies and social education agencies. The impression of the inspection was very good. The educational administration in the province is well-organized, the order is stable, the educational funding is independent, and there are many primary and secondary schools and social education agencies. The examination system is very thorough and commendable. Primary and secondary schools not only have graduation examinations, but also have an examination at the end of each academic year.

Henan University Students Come to Beijing to Petition

New President Zhang Guangyu Goes to Bian to Take Office and Expresses Opinions

(Nanjing, 30th) The Ministry of Education previously ordered the political science department of Henan University to stop enrolling students. The students of the university plan to request the revocation of the order and have sent representatives to petition the Henan Provincial Government. The result was satisfactory. On the 30th, they sent representatives to Beijing to petition the Ministry of Education. Shen Pengfei met with them and expressed sympathy for the students' requests and agreed to submit them to the minister.

The newly appointed president of Henan University, Zhang Guangyu, went to Bian from Beijing on the 28th to take office. Zhang is currently the director of general affairs at Central University. Before this, President Luo of Central University had earnestly tried to persuade him to stay, but Zhang had to refuse because of the strong pressure from Henan and his duty to his hometown. Before leaving, he said that he had once been the president of the university in 1920 and had detailed plans to promote school affairs, but he had left the school due to changes in the political situation, which had not been realized. This time, he will strictly implement the Ministry of Education's order to rectify higher education, improve the students' level, enrich the content of the departments, hire excellent teachers, and increase the number of books and equipment, so that Henan University will gradually develop into a well-known university in the country. However, Henan University is short of funds and it is difficult to operate. This time, he is determined to work hard for the academic community, regardless of personal sacrifice.

Local

Students Who Fail One or Two Subjects in the Examination Will Not Be Allowed to Advance

Ministry of Education Responds to the Municipal Education Association

The Ministry of Education's examination regulations stipulate that students who fail one or two subjects in the examination will not be allowed to advance. In order to prevent students from wasting their studies, the Municipal Education Association has sent a telegram to the Ministry of Education requesting that these students be temporarily allowed to advance as special students. It is now learned that the Ministry of Education has replied to the association that high school students who fail one or two subjects in the examination must take remedial classes in accordance with the regulations and will not be allowed to advance. Junior high school students may take the entrance examination for higher education with equivalent academic ability, but will not be allowed to advance with graduation qualifications.

▲ The Municipal Education Bureau Will Formulate a Unified Standard

▲ To be Announced and Implemented After Approval by the Municipal Government

The treatment of teachers and staff in municipal and rural district elementary schools in this city has not been uniform. Teachers and staff in rural district elementary schools have proposed unified treatment. It is now learned that the Municipal Education Bureau has formulated a unified standard for the treatment of teachers and staff in municipal and rural districts starting in 1933 and will announce and implement it after it is approved by the Municipal Government and the Ministry of Education.

The Chinese Education Society Held a Board Meeting Yesterday

△ Resolved to Request Administrative Agencies to Subsidize Experimental Work Expenses

△ Joined the World Education Society and Nominated Ai Wei to Attend

△ Continued Meeting This Morning to Discuss Education Undertakings

South African Fauchier, who defeated Britain's top player Pennell on Tuesday, unexpectedly lost in straight sets to Czechoslovakian Davis Cup player Menuel. Both men's and women's singles players have been reduced to sixteen. Barnes decisively defeated Japan's Miki in straight sets.

▲ Fauchier also Eliminated

The young South African Cambridge student Fauchier, after defeating Pennell, lost without a fight to Czechoslovakia's Menuel. Fauchier completely lost the form he had on Tuesday, losing in straight sets, 6-3, 6-3, 6-2.

▲ Barnes Overwhelms Miki

Champion Barnes effortlessly advanced to the fourth week, overwhelmingly defeating Japan's Miki, known as the "dark horse," in straight sets, 6-2, 6-4, 6-4. Barnes is improving match by match, just like last year. His victory over Miki was impressive. Miki's high balls were completely controlled by Barnes' smashes. Miki's mistake was also relying too much on high balls, failing to recognize Barnes' excellent overhead smashes.
