Strange Developments in the Boxing World

Former World Heavyweight Champion

Sharkey Suddenly Knocked Out

Canera's Amazing Feat

(New York, 29th) The world of heavyweight boxing is full of twists and turns. German master Schmeling was defeated by the American Max Baer, and now Italian giant Canera knocked out former champion Sharkey in the sixth round of a fifteen-round match. The heavyweight championship crown will now go to either Max Baer or Canera.

▲ The blast erupts, Italian Canera weighs 18 pounds and eight and a half ounces (each pound equals fourteen pounds), Sharkey only fourteen pounds five, a difference of more than fifty pounds. The contest was extremely heated. The outcome felt like a giant bomb exploding among the 40,000 spectators, leaving them in shock.

▲ Sharkey Falls and Cannot Rise, Sharkey had won the first five rounds, victory seemed to be in his grasp, but Canera unleashed all his strength, striking his opponent, then using his frighteningly short arms to strike upwards, Sharkey swayed and fell, unable to rise. This is his third defeat in his life.

▲ Punching the Opponent's Jaw, In the first round, Canera charged from the corner, looking excited. Sharkey lunged into the ring, hitting the opponent with a series of left punches. The Italian retaliated, driving Sharkey to the ropes. Sharkey then hit the opponent's head from the left, right and center. Before the first bell rang, the American's right hand landed squarely on Canera's jaw.

▲ Staggering by the Ropes, In the second round, the Italian acted cautiously, swinging his long arms. Sharkey's breathing became constricted. But he returned with a punch to the jaw, as heavy as a thousand pounds. Canera staggered by the ropes. The American intended to continue his advance, but suddenly came under attack himself, and could not proceed due to labored breathing. The second round ended there.

▲ Forced to Defend, In the third round, Sharkey remained calm, feinting attacks to confuse the opponent, hitting the head and body repeatedly. Canera was forced to defend under pressure.

▲ Warning for Foul Play, In the fourth round, the giant's left arm stretched out, suddenly hitting Sharkey, making him lose his balance. Fortunately, he was not injured due to proper handling. The Italian missed many opportunities at this time, and suddenly hooked Sharkey's left hand, pulling him closer, while repeatedly striking his head. The referee immediately issued a warning for this foul play.

▲ Swaying Back to Position, In the fifth round, Sharkey was about to take advantage of a moment of weakness when the Italian repeated his previous mistake, receiving another warning. The American attacked Canera forcefully. Before the bell rang, the Italian was punched and swayed back to his corner.

▲ Successful Blow, In the sixth round, Sharkey first hit the opponent's face, then struck his body. Canera retaliated, driving the champion back. Suddenly, he slipped, but immediately sprang up. Canera advanced with both left and right punches. Sharkey was struck and fell to the ground. The count of ten was over, and Sharkey still did not rise. The outcome was decided. The end of the round was two minutes and twenty-seven seconds.

Primer on Transmitters

— Jiancun

▲：：：：：▲

2. Elements of a Transmitter

To understand the internal structure of a transmitter, one must first understand the general elements that make up a transmitter. The main elements are shown in the first diagram, and are described in detail below.

[Diagram 1]

Radio wave Antenna Ground Electrical Amplifier Oscillator Modulator Sound Amplifier Sound wave

(1) Microphone: A microphone is a device that converts sound waves, music, and other sound waves into electrical current. The current generated by the microphone changes according to changes in sound wave pressure. This type of current is commonly referred to as sound current.

(2) Sound Amplifier: The sound current generated by the microphone is extremely weak and must be amplified to an appropriate level by a sound amplifier before being sent to the modulator.

(3) Oscillator: An oscillator is used to generate an oscillating current of a certain frequency. The frequency of this oscillating current determines the wavelength of the radio wave emitted by the antenna. For example, the frequency of the Nanjing Central Broadcasting Station is 680 kHz, and the converted wavelength of the emitted radio wave is 440 meters.

(4) Modulator: The function of the modulator is to synthesize the oscillating current and the sound current to generate a radio frequency current that can be emitted by the antenna. In other words, it changes the oscillating current into the waveform of the sound current.

(5) Power Amplifier: The modulated current after modulation is amplified to an appropriate level by the power amplifier and then emitted by the antenna.

(6) Antenna: Finally, the modulated current, which has been amplified to an appropriate level, is converted into a radio wave and emitted into space. This is the function of the antenna.

Simplified Wavelength Calculation Method

— Chen Ren

The usual method for calculating wavelength is to use the following formula:

λ = 1884√(LC)

λ is the wavelength (in meters), L is the inductance (in millihenries), and C is the capacitance (in microfarads).

For example, if you have a 0.0005 µF capacitor and a 73 µH coil, to find the wavelength:

λ = 1884√(73 * 0.0005) = 359.8 meters

Now, if we know the product of L and C required for a certain wavelength, then it is very easy to find L or C. The table is as follows:

Wavelength Frequency Product of Inductance and Capacitance (i.e., L x C)

200 1.500 0.01129

220 1.363 0.01362

240 1.250 0.01623

260 1.154 0.01902

280 1.071 0.02209

300 1.000 0.02530

320 0.937 0.02884

340 0.882 0.03249

360 0.833 0.03648

380 0.789 0.04070

400 0.750 0.04507

420 0.714 0.04970

440 0.682 0.05446

According to the above table, if you want to receive a wavelength of 360 meters and you have a 0.00025 mfd capacitor, to find the size of the coil to use, simply divide the product of inductance and capacitance (i.e., LC) by 0.00025. According to the table above, the LC for a wavelength of 360 is 0.03648. Divide 0.03648 by 0.00025 and you get 146.

If you have a 146 microhenry coil, to find the capacitance of the capacitor, simply divide 0.03648 by 146, which gives you 0.00025.

Radio World Personalities

Sommering

丨Inventor of Using Waterways to Replace Cables丨

Sommering was a German, born in 1755, who was a famous scientist when he died. While studying telegraphy, he thought of using waterways to replace cables and carried out his famous experiment. During the experiment, the current was interrupted due to incomplete equipment, and he made an incorrect judgment, believing that his ideal was impractical, which is a pity! Although his experiment was not continued, it did advance the practical methods of radio, which is noteworthy. The world's verdict on Sommering is:

"A person who sincerely loves science and is dedicated to public welfare."

Radio Common Sense

— Huang Jiancun

(9) Coils

(1) Nature of Coils: In the radio world, the term "coil" should be called a self-inductance coil, but for the sake of brevity, it is simply called a coil. Any wire wound on a suitable frame can be called a coil. Some have iron cores, and some do not. In diagrams, a coil without an iron core is often represented by, and a coil with an iron core is represented by or . Both have self-inductance to resist alternating current. The greater the self-inductance, the smaller the alternating current passing through the coil, and the strength of the resistance varies with the size of the alternating current frequency. Generally, the higher the frequency, the stronger the resistance. This special resistance of the coil to alternating current is called reactance. This relationship can be expressed by the following formula. Let L be the self-inductance of the coil, be the frequency, and be the circumference ratio, i.e. 3.1416, then

Resistance = 2 × × Frequency × Self-Inductance = fL

(2) Unit: The unit of self-inductance in a coil is the henry (HenIy), abbreviated as h. However, in radio, the value of the henry is sometimes too large, so one thousandth of 1h is often used as a unit, called millihenry, abbreviated as m. Or one millionth is used as a unit, called microhenry, abbreviated as ub. Namely:

1h = 1000mh = 1,000,000uh

The self-inductance of a coil varies with its shape, number of turns, and the presence or absence of an iron core. Generally, the larger the shape of the coil and the more turns, the greater the self-inductance.

(3) Types of Coils: There are many types of coils used in the radio world. The most commonly used ones are shown in the following figure. In the figure, (1) is a spider web coil, (2) is a cylindrical coil, (3) is a honeycomb coil, (4) is a cage coil, and (5) is a stacked coil.

(4) Wire Used for Coils: At present, the copper wire used for coils is mostly silk-covered or yarn-covered wire from No. 10 to No. 30. It is difficult to say which number of copper wire is most suitable. If the diameter of the copper wire used is large, the consumption resistance is less, but the coil made is often too large, so generally No. 22 to No. 30 is the most suitable.

The size of copper wire is expressed by numbers. There are two standards for expressing the number of copper wire, one is the American standard, abbreviated as B.S., and the other is the British standard, abbreviated as B.W.G.

Announcement by the Radio Weekly Department of Shen Bao

Page 22

Free Talk

Starting with a Headache

— Xie Bingying

Ever since I saw the "Talk more about romance, less about complaints" notice from the Free Talk editor, I've had a headache that hasn't stopped. The doctor told me that headaches are a sign of neurasthenia. To prevent headaches, don't use your mind. The best thing to do is to find friends to chat with or go out to play after eating every day. If you're tired, go to sleep. If you wake up hungry, eat something. After eating, go out to play or chat again. In short, live a pig-like life of "being full all day and doing nothing." Heaven! How can I do that? Not only do my life and work not allow me to not work, but even if my body gets two days of rest temporarily, it is absolutely impossible to prevent my brain from thinking in an hour.

"Unless you cut off my head, there's no way to stop me from thinking!" I protested to the doctor one day very seriously.

"May I ask what good is it to use your brain all day long?" He also questioned me seriously.

"Who cares if it's good or bad, anyway, she wants to think, what can I do?"

"Okay, then don't complain about headaches and insomnia in the future, and don't come to see me often."

That's it, now I don't even dare to tell the doctor that I'm sick.

○○○○

I'm more of a talkative and complaining person, which is mostly due to the promotion of the environment, but now I'm encountering an extremely silent life. Although friends often write to encourage me to write something, I feel that if this continues, I won't even be able to write a letter in the future. I really want to take the opportunity to cheer myself up with someone urging me, but what to write? Not only can I not participate in national affairs, but it is impossible to even talk about them, so what else can I write? I can't write or want to write about romance, suicide, and love, so what else can I write?

I remember when Mr. Li Liewen first took over the editorship of Free Talk, I was very enthusiastic and got a few things done in those days. Someone asked me, "You've written a lot of things recently!" I replied to him: "Not really, but because it's Free Talk, I'm happy to have a free talk."

But what about now? The word "no" has to be added to "Free Talk," so what else can we write?

Someone wrote to me and said: "Now the misfortune of Chinese writers has arrived. If they can only make a living by selling articles, they can only wait to die." I wrote back to him and said: "If they don't think of a way to break out of a new path, it's best to dig their graves first and crawl into the ground."

Friends who are engaged in writing, what are you going to do? June 18, 1933, in Long

Looking at "The Big Parade"

— Cao Juren

It seems the Second World War is about to begin, and like a lesson to be reviewed, we need to re-examine the scene of 1914. We squeezed among the foreign soldiers, watching the performance of "The Big Parade"; what was projected onto my heart was the giant's hairy palm, making me tremble and filling me with awe at the unknowable destiny!

The scene of the soldiers' jubilation on the battlefield when the armistice news arrived moved me deeply. But what happened after returning from the battlefield? Like the fate of the free farmers of Rome, "Having fulfilled his duty to the country, he went out to fight for his country without complaint; after ten, fifteen, twenty years, he returned home, his land overgrown with weeds, and his home ruined. Nevertheless, he was willing to start all over again. He tilled the land, sowed the seeds, and hoped for a harvest. He took his grain, cattle, sheep, ducks, and chickens to the market, but there were many large landowners who used slaves to cultivate the land, deliberately depreciating the prices of all goods, so he suffered great losses. For two years, he could still maintain his own livelihood. But later, he was desperate and had to abandon his land. He left the countryside and came to the nearest city. He was starving in the city, just as he had been in the fields. But there was no other way but to endure the same suffering as thousands of other landless poor people. They all squatted in dilapidated houses outside the city, making them easily susceptible to infectious diseases and death. They went out to fight for their country, but received such a reward in return." (Hendrik Willem van Loon, *The Story of Mankind*)

Therefore, the sharp call to arms caused millions of prospective widows and orphans to crowd the stations; the bugle call caused millions of strong young men to fall crippled and broken on the trenches; where the forty-two centimeter guns passed, tall buildings turned to ashes; airplanes circled over the city of Paris, frightening men and women in the streets to scatter like birds and beasts; the battlefield hospitals could not treat the wounded soldiers in time, leaving them to writhe and scream to death; each of these scenes was a heartbreaking tragedy; but thinking of starving to death in the city, these lives cut short seemed much happier.

A friend who hurriedly shaved his beard upon hearing the armistice news, recalling Wilson's speech in Washington about fighting for peace, and generously enlisting in the army, could not help but laugh at himself. But when he joined the breadline and stepped into Washington to petition, recalling that he hurriedly shaved his beard upon hearing the armistice news, he could not help but laugh at himself again.

However, humanity is always forgetful. The crippled and broken have died one after another, and there are those who are preparing to sacrifice themselves on the battlefield for a speech. The performance of "The Big Parade" is precisely a suggestion of this serious epoch!

The Neighbors

— Peng Jiahuan

When I knocked on the back door at eleven o'clock that night, I saw a friend from the small room next door also knocking on the door. He knocked so rhythmically and gently, calling out, "Mom of so-and-so, please open the door!" His head was looking up at the dark and cold small room. Naturally, so was I.

We began to wander under the window. Although we didn't talk, our hearts were well aware of each other's troubles.

Instead of hearing footsteps on the stairs, someone came downstairs. My back door suddenly opened with a bang, like a scene from an empty fort strategy. What could be said in the middle of the night? Prepare for total annihilation, that's all. Embracing the spirit of sacrifice, I walked in blankly. Trembling and shrinking beside the sleeping child, my heart was breaking as I thought about the failure of the day's efforts, especially the fear that I would be torn apart by harsh words and venomous tongues. I couldn't help but concentrate and forget myself, forgetting everything close to me, to listen to the commotion in the small room next door. I believed that was the best way to deal with me.

The woman's voice kept coming from the small room next door:

"You wild thing, did you go out to borrow money? You wild boar! You have to come home at this hour to borrow money!"

"Hey, I'm asking you, I'm asking you, you borrowed money, you borrowed money, where is the money? Hurry up and give it to me, you dead man!"

"Oh, you spend the whole day playing outside, letting your wife and children eat gruel at home, are you human! Are you human! You pig, you dirty thing. If you have the guts, die outside and never come back!"

"This kind of man, huh, I've never seen such a man, useless, can't earn any money! And you pretend to be stupid, saying you have a place to borrow money, a place to borrow money, borrowing until midnight, how much did you borrow?"

"Dead man, bring it here, you won't bring it? Okay, okay, I want to see what you can do. I don't want to live like this anymore..."

Just as I was listening intently, suddenly my hair was pulled:

"Ghost, ghost, you think it's okay if you don't say anything, you think it's okay if you don't say anything! Humph, you think I'm an easy target, just wait, tomorrow, I'll tell on you..."

"I'm sorry, I'm sorry, I was listening to the noise in the small room next door, I'm sorry."

I couldn't help but listen to the commotion in the small room next door, because it was the best way to deal with me. I thought the friend in the small room next door must be the same as me, because I never heard a sound from him.

Respectful Reply to Mr. He Ru

— Luo Fu

My "Further Explanation" was to avoid the suspicion of differing opinions, not to boast of unique insights, nor to risk being considered stale talk. If Mr. He Ru wants to seek the sword from the boat from this point, I admit that my wording is clumsy. Even if it is said to be "the Three Character Classic," if there is no respect between us, there is no need for dissatisfaction. Like my reply today, it is also "the Three Character Classic," because they are all "common knowledge." But it is not "casual writing, nor is it playing with things and neglecting one's duties." At least, it can "help to trace the historical origins," so it will not "misoccupy space" or "waste time." This is what I want to "solemnly declare."

The roles in Peking Opera are divided into civil and military, such as *Sheng* and *Wu Sheng*, *Xiao Sheng* and *Wu Xiao Sheng*, *Dan* and *Wu Dan*, *Chou* and *Wu Chou*, and there are also some roles that are both civil and military. But in Kun Opera, only some *Xiao Sheng* or *Sheng* wear military attire, and there is no title of *Wu Sheng*. The same is true for *Wu Dan*; for example, Wu Song in *The Tale of the Righteous Knight* is played by *Xiao Sheng*, and Gu Dasao is played by *Dan*. Yi Zhangqing is played by *Xiao Dan*, which is a good example. As for *Wu Chou*, it has existed in Peking Opera for a hundred years, but there is no precedent for even *Dao* roles in Kun Opera.

Because Kun Opera does not have military plays. In plays such as *Romance of the Three Kingdoms* and *Water Margin*, when it comes to fighting, it is just a scene change, not a big fight. As for somersaults and tiger leaps, Kun Opera would not have them. Therefore, there is no need to specially set up military roles.

The existence of military plays affects the music of the play. Like the music section of Peking Opera; commonly known as the stage, the stage is divided into civil and military stages. The large cymbals and drums are the military stage, and the *erhu*, *yueqin*, flute, and *sheng* are all the civil stage. The main music of Kun Opera is the *guan* and flute. The main music of the earlier Yiyang Opera and Kunshan Opera was the *suo*. Later, the main music of Chongyang Opera, Siyang Opera, and Qin Opera was the same. Only Gaoqiang does not use string and wind instruments together, only using gongs and drums. Except for this exception, the main instruments in the singing and dancing stage, besides string instruments, wind instruments, and percussion instruments, are still only drums and clappers, which is the civil stage of Eastern Opera. The scene of large cymbals and drums is to help the fighting, and only after military plays flourished did it have its path to find.

During the Qing dynasty, when the emperor returned to the palace after the winter solstice suburban sacrifice, there was a kind of ceremonial dance performed by the actors of the imperial theater from top to bottom, each receiving one tael of silver. This shows that somersaults and tiger leaps were originally a kind of street performance, and the music of the military stage was to boost the prestige of the street performance, it was the scene of the street performance. Later, the street performance and the old opera merged, and this scene also merged with the scene of the civil stage.

According to Gu [?], feats like tumbling were interspersed between civil stage dramas in the Ming dynasty, that is, they were not integrated into the drama. Instead, they were performed in the interlude between the end of play A and the beginning of play B to create a lively atmosphere. The music for this lively atmosphere was of course large cymbals and drums, but whether it was play A or play B, they were all civil stages. I have not missed anything except this.

But Mr. He Ru said, "Tumbling cannot be mixed with northern tunes, but there are military movements without cymbals and drums." This is because he did not "look closely at the following text," so he "cannot help but be disappointed." I have never said that "northern tunes have military movements"; I only said that military movements were not formally integrated into northern tunes, so the military stage with large cymbals and drums was also not formally integrated into northern tunes, and the earliest southern tunes were no exception. Therefore, regarding this point, I also "cannot agree and respectfully return it."

However, I boldly accept Mr. He Ru's generous gift. Because I advocate that "cymbals and drums and military movements simultaneously invaded old operas," but I do not acknowledge the "Three Character Classic" that "ever since there was such a thing as drama, it has never been separated from cymbals and drums," because I would not call wild street dances drama, and at least, spoken drama does not use cymbals and drums, which everyone should acknowledge.

Regarding "Big Face," I didn't say much because of the word count; I hope Mr. He Ru can continue to find "the musical instruments accompanied by Big Face singing and dancing" and quickly break out of the scope of "I guess."

Carrot Top

— Jules Renard, translated by Lin Qu

Carrot Top's Photo Album (Continued)

Fourteen

"Spoiling! What does that mean?" Carrot Top asked Little Pierre, who was pampered by his mother.

After roughly understanding what it was about, he exclaimed:

"As for me, what I hope is to dip my fingers in the leftover fried sweet potato crumbs in the pot again and suck on the half of the peach with the pit."

He thought for a moment:

"If Mrs. Lepic gives me affectionate caresses, she will definitely start with the abacus beads."

Fifteen

Sometimes, sister Ernestine and brother Felix, tired of playing, voluntarily lent their toys to Carrot Top. He took a portion of each of their happiness and humbly put together his own happiness.

Because he was afraid they would ask him to return them, he dared not show that he was happy.

Sixteen

Carrot Top: So, don't you think my ears are too long?

Mathilde: I think your ears are very strange; would you lend them to me? I want to fill them with some sand to play with desserts.

Carrot Top: If Mom burns them first, the sand will be roasted in there.

Seventeen

"Won't you stop? Let me hear it again! So, between me and your father, who do you like more?" Mrs. Lepic said everywhere.

"I stand still, I don't say anything, I can swear to you, I don't like either of you," Carrot Top answered in his heart.

Eighteen

Mrs. Lepic: What are you doing, Carrot Top?

Carrot Top: I don't know, Mom.

Mrs. Lepic: That means you're doing something unconsciously again. Are you doing it on purpose?

Carrot Top: That's the only thing I lack.

Nineteen

Carrot Top thought his mother was smiling at him, very happy, so he smiled along.

But Mrs. Lepic, who was vaguely smiling to herself, suddenly turned her face stern, like a black wooden head with two black raspberry-like eyes embedded in it.

Flustered, Carrot Top didn't know where to run.

Spring and Autumn

Human Misfortune

— Xianxian

Whether "science" will be "beneficial" or "harmful" to the future life of mankind is a mystery that even Liu Bowen reborn or Zhuge Liang resurrected would find difficult to "foresee."

"Telephones" inevitably require switchboard operators. However, after telephone companies upgraded to "automatic telephones," the "rice bowls" of a large number of switchboard operators have become a pile of "broken pieces."

In the past, in the early morning and evening, we could often see male and female workers from various factories riding "wheelbarrows" back and forth. Since the advent of "fast, cheap, and accessible" trams, the "wheelbarrows" have changed from transporting "people" to mainly transporting "goods." But now, larger companies and firms have their own "trucks for transporting goods," and the lives of "wheelbarrow pullers" are gradually approaching "the setting sun."

"Foreign cloth" is not only delicate and smooth but also cheap. Therefore, farmers in rural China who grow their own cotton and weave their own cloth can only carry the cloth to the city and back home, worrying about the rice jar. After the invention of scientific dyeing and weaving methods, the Chinese silk industry plummeted, and silk workers experienced great panic.

The Indian national father Mahatma Gandhi advocated "homespun cloth" and cursed "science," which seemed to be reversing the trend of the times. But if we put aside the pleasures of "wine" and "meat" and think deeply, if some "scientific product" were to take away the work you rely on to earn bread, then what would your "life" be like? Even if you have a "scientific mind," you can't help but doubt "science."

This is not a joke. According to the current "rate of scientific progress," any complex task can be performed by things without "nerves." For example, the police officers who manage "vehicle traffic" at intersections can reportedly be replaced by custom-made "puppets."

"Robots" can already fly airplanes, safely flying from Los Angeles to New York. With this kind of evolution, is there still a "way out" for humanity? Although we are now enjoying a lot of benefits from "science," the "misfortune" of mankind is probably about to come!

Summer Night in the Park

— Huang Kewei

The gentle evening breeze took away the heat of the early summer in this southern country. The park, shrouded in the golden setting sun, was filled with a sweet atmosphere.

Trees stretched out their arms, standing like a green gauze umbrella. Birds chirped and sang, fluttering their clever tongues, red, black, yellow... Wildflowers, revealing their fresh and delicate beauty, secretly peeked at the naked thighs in the long cheongsams.

There were passionate Parisian girls, red jackets, white short skirts, golden hair, dancing with flowing sleeves. There were petite Japanese girls, three or four with high buns, white necks, and colorful clothes, with a bright bag on their shoulders, wooden clogs clattering in symphony. There were Indian women, wearing long shawls that reached the ground, large breasts shaking in their loose clothing, earrings, rings, bracelets, flashing golden light, descendants of the noble titles of a fallen kingdom!

Young people held the white, tender, round arms of modern girls, their long trousers lightly passing over the green grass. The wind carried the fragrance of their lover's flesh and powder, kissing the faces of the young people, their feathery steps treading lightly, circling along the grassy path, or sitting under the green shade, talking and laughing, happy, without worry, without pain!

The ice cream shop was temporarily decorated in a modern style, like prostitutes who put on makeup and go out to sell their bodies at night. The waiters put on brand-new uniforms, smiling and waiting for customers.

The music pavilion shone with white-hot lights, the large bass drum raising its hoarse voice, roughly, harmonizing with the other musical sounds, playing a summer tune.

The moon had just risen from the east, faintly, the night shrouded the entire garden, blurring all the outlines, only the delicate laughter still rippled in the sparsely moonlit green shade.

— Geng Bai

A path through the woods is right at the door, the flowers and plants are sparse and the mood is naturally warm. It is not necessary to seek coolness, the snowy sky and moonlit ground doubles the dissipation of melancholy.

From afar, I hear the sound of a sawing board, like the rustling of wind and waves. The birds sing in the deep shade of the tung trees, who knows my feelings at this moment? (Last line borrowed)

The golden land needs rain, walking can make [?]

The mood is special. The sense of poverty and wealth comes and goes in my heart, and I have not burned the book due to the unfair climate.

There is also gentle wave with green shade, sunset like an orange the writing has just begun to sink. But I seek the taste of Xuanwu Lake, washing away the heart of the traveler day and night.

Why does the wind cicada bring sorrow, small years and shallow waves. It seems that my focus is a mistake, there is not much to say in the world.

Four people strolled leisurely in pairs, dancing pavilions and sparse fences on both sides of the shore. Clearly seen are the new [?] artifacts, ten thousand crows writing Shenzhou like ink!

Robot Sketches

— Hutou

I had just written this topic when a friend next to me laughed and said: "What is there to sketch about robots? They always get off at the New World, like the clerks of the Three Companies. There is also a Frenchman who, when he gets on the car, looks around, first at the people in the car, as if to prevent pickpockets, after looking around, he sits down with his butt. He is not a clerk of the tram company, but a figure from the police station, because he never buys a ticket and sits in the first class. There used to be a large group of different people getting on at the Father Raos Station, but recently there are very few, sometimes even no one. The reason is that the houses are being rebuilt at Father Raos West Street, and these robots may have moved. Going north along the road is Rue Lafayette. At the intersection of Chengyu Lane, there is a modern miss, about seventeen or eighteen years old, who always gets on the car with a mister around thirty years old. It is not clear whether it is a black lacquered bench or what. Listening to their conversation, the girl is studying at the Nanyang Senior Commercial School, and the man slips away alone at the north end of the Great World. Recently, another miss in a blue cheongsam has been added to the Rue Lafayette station, with small eyes, and dimples on her face, often reflecting, especially when she opens her mouth to laugh. At the Taipingqiao station, there is a woman in her thirties and a pitifully thin man. This woman has a shiny bun and carries a paper bag in her hand, like a student's homework, getting on the car obediently, without any playful expression, and it is clear at a glance that she is a teacher somewhere. There is also a pitifully thin man, like my classmate, but I still can't be sure, so I have never greeted him; sometimes he wears a suit, sometimes he wears a long gown. Looking at his face, it seems that he has severe lung disease, if not the third stage, then the second stage, but he is still engaged in the robot life. From here to Cale Road, and Nanyang Bridge [?]. Why do you have to rack your brains to earn a few manuscript fees? This is really unnecessary, unnecessary!" I said: "Wait, wait! The robots I am talking about are not made of wood, nor are they made by machines, but their work and rest are at a certain time, like a machine that is wound up and always moves accordingly, and they are still people with flesh and blood and bones. Therefore, the 'Robot Sketches' are sketches of all kinds of people." [title explanation]

Those of us live a dull life every day, which is very boring. But one thing is also very interesting, that is, many people will meet you at the same time without prior arrangement. Although they are all strangers, they seem to have become acquaintances just because they meet every day. So I have the need to describe each of the unfamiliar him and her.

I live in Xieqiao, Nanshi, and work in Meibaige Road. Trolleybus No. 18 is my good friend "I can't live without this gentleman" . Along the way with me: there are misses, there are also misters. I take the bus around 8:30 in the morning. At the same time, two or three people get on at Kangti Road, one is a miss in a fashionable cheongsam, not very high heels, with a thin layer of powder on her face. No, Zhujiaqiao, Ningbo Road, Baxianqiao, Great World: although people get on and off, there is no certainty, so they cannot be regarded as robots. Probably this area is a display of fleshy bodies, the place of origin of waxberries, so robots are not worthy of living in it.

The Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Ten

Hearing the words, Fangxin was shocked that the wish to be ennobled was distant

Listening to the song, he envied the color and leisurely served the country

Mr. Niu, you tell me, marrying such a soldier, am I enjoying happiness while he is alive? Or am I enjoying happiness after he dies? He left behind two boys and one girl, and I have to raise them. Over the years, not to mention the clothes and food for myself and the children, I also have to provide for the children to study. What am I marrying a husband for? It is simply paying off debts from a previous life. Guizhi couldn't help but gasp in her heart after hearing what he said. So this is the fate of marrying a soldier. Sitting on the kang, pressing her hands on the kang mat, she stared at Aunt Liu's face, stunned. Mr. Niu also pressed his hands on his knees, looking at Aunt Liu's face, shaking his head a few times and saying, "Suddenly seeing the willow color at the head of the tomb, regretting teaching my husband to seek nobility." As the saying goes, "Don't laugh at me drunk on the battlefield, how many have returned from ancient battles?" Guizhi and Aunt Liu didn't understand what he was saying and didn't pay attention to him. Mr. Niu was feeling awkward because someone was complaining to him, so he said to Aunt Liu, "Sister-in-law, did you ask me to come here to say something?" Aunt Liu exclaimed, laughed, and said, "Look, I'm just talking and delaying the serious business." As she said this, she sighed again, "To tell you the truth, this child's father, although we were separated more than we met, we had a very good relationship. Tomorrow is his birthday, I always remember. When I think of his good points, I want to burn two paper packages for him. I'm asking you for nothing else, just to write two paper package covers." The more Guizhi heard these words, the more she felt creepy. These words were nothing but more and more unbearable to hear. She really didn't want to listen anymore, so she said, "Aunt Liu, I have something to do, I don't want to sit anymore, please give me the pills." Aunt Liu didn't dare to keep her for long because the woman's mother was sick, so she had to give her the pills and let her go back. Guizhi walked home, her face was unusually pale. Without saying a word, she put the small package of pills she brought back on the table. Seeing the clothes her mother hadn't finished making on the kang, she picked up the needle and thread and sat down to start sewing. (116)
